The Chinese side has commissioned the Star Film Company to film, while the foreign side will be filmed by the American Fox Film Corporation.

Yu Hongjun Discusses Autonomy Preparation

Retrenchment is Temporary, Slightly Relieving Financial Strength

The Situation is Slightly Stable, Actively Proceeding

Central News Agency reports: The Shanghai Municipal Autonomy Preparatory Committee, after being ordered to retrench following the 236th municipal administration meeting of the Municipal Government last week, caused many outside to be unclear about the truth, leading to much speculation, with some even saying that this retrenchment meant suspension of the committee. Opinions differed, and no consensus was reached. For this reason, this reporter went to the Municipal Government to interview Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, who kindly spoke in detail. Mr. Yu's remarks are recorded below. The preparations for local autonomy in various provinces and cities are a crucial task that the central government has limited time to complete during the tutelage period. Shanghai's special status is of great importance. Since receiving the central government's order in the 19th year (of the Republic), the city first established the Shanghai Municipal Local Autonomy Training Institute to cultivate a large number of specialized autonomy talents for local use. At the same time, the Shanghai Municipal Government's Municipal District Division Committee was established to investigate the city's district boundaries, dividing the 13 administrative districts into 40 autonomous districts. After years of work, the foundation for autonomy was completed. Subsequently, the city was planning to continue carrying out household surveys and dividing neighborhoods to facilitate the election of autonomy officials at all levels, but the January 28th Incident happened at that time. The Municipal Government's established steps had to be temporarily suspended. When the Shanghai war ended in May of last year and an agreement was reached, the Municipal Government, on July 1st of the same year, organized the Shanghai Municipal Autonomy Preparatory Committee to take charge of the unfinished matters of the previous District Division Committee. The former District Division Committee was only in charge of the district division, which was the beginning of the autonomy preparation. The Autonomy Preparatory Committee is responsible for the entire preparation task. The complexity is self-evident. Therefore, the organization was specially augmented to facilitate progress. Within a month of the committee's establishment, all the articles of association were drafted and reported, and the entire preparation was divided into three periods: preparation, investigation, and election. From July 1st of last year to June 31st of this year, within one year, the city's autonomy preparation was to be completed, and the elected district offices and all levels of autonomous organs of the municipal organization law were to be established. In July of last year, when the January 28th Incident had just ended in the city and the local area suffered greatly, the Municipal Government established the committee amid efforts to prepare for local post-war recovery and relief, showing its emphasis on the matter and its willingness to do its utmost. The original plan submitted by the committee stipulated that the district offices should be established by August 31st of last year. At that time, the selection of district chiefs and the Municipal Government's financial resources were not something that could be done hastily. Therefore, it was delayed until December of last year that the appointed district chiefs were approved by the Ministry of Interior and reported to the Executive Yuan for record. Then the committee re-planned and decided to start the organization from January 1st of this year, postponing the original deadline for the establishment of the district offices by half a year. Unexpectedly, before long, the war in North China suddenly broke out. The whole country was affected by the increasing foreign aggression, even in daily administration. How much more so for this important autonomy task, which was hoped for by both the upper and lower levels and related to the foundation of Shanghai for generations to come? How could it be done hastily in the midst of this national crisis? This was due to the circumstances, and it was necessary to wait for an opportunity to proceed. In the middle of last month, the Municipal Government, due to the current lack of financial resources and the impact of the situation, which would not be easy to recover in the short term, received a request from the committee for instructions, which was submitted to the 236th Municipal Administration Meeting. It was decided to temporarily retrench, and at the same time report to the Executive Yuan for approval. The purpose of the retrenchment was only to reduce the expenses of the committee and slightly relieve the financial resources, while the Autonomy Preparatory Committee would still exist, and the members would continue to plan. On the one hand, they would quietly wait for instructions from the Executive Yuan. In short, the Municipal Government has long been determined to quickly complete the preparation for local autonomy in Shanghai, as can be seen from the efforts to establish the Autonomy Preparatory Committee after the war last year. As long as the circumstances permit, every effort will be made. As for empty talk and wild speculation, that is not known.

Page 14

The Extraterritorial Road Construction Case Will Have New Developments

The Specific Nature is Still Unclear

Guowen News Agency reports: The extraterritorial roads built by the Public Concession had been negotiated for recovery last year by Mr. Yu Hongjun, Secretary-General of our Municipal Government, and Mr. Fessenden, Director-General of the Public Works Department, and there was hope for a solution. However, due to obstruction from the Japanese side, the case has been delayed until now for more than half a year. Recently, there is hope for continued negotiations. The history of the case and recent news are recorded as follows.

Negotiation Process

Mr. Yu Hongjun, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, acting on the instructions of the Municipal Government and the Executive Yuan, and Mr. Fessenden, Director-General of the Public Works Department, acting on the instructions of the Board of Directors of the Public Works Department, held consultations back and forth, and their opinions were quite close. A draft agreement was also drafted, detailing the administrative issues of recovering the extraterritorial roads. Both parties separately requested instructions from their competent authorities. The Executive Yuan requested the original text of the draft agreement reported by the Municipal Government and instructed that the wording be revised. After receiving the order, Secretary Yu consulted with Mr. Fessenden again. The Public Works Department also intended to accommodate our amendments to the wording. Unexpectedly, at this time, the Japanese side obstructed the process with various demands, causing it to be delayed indefinitely.

Japanese Obstruction

The Japanese opposition to our country's recovery of the extraterritorial roads was initially expressed by Japanese directors Terai and Okamoto at the Board of Directors of the Public Works Department. However, because the majority of the directors from various countries supported the return to our country, the Japanese directors' opposition failed as an absolute minority in the Board of Directors. They then changed their tactics and had the Japanese Consul-General in Shanghai, Ishii Jūtaro, negotiate with the Public Works Department. Mr. Fessenden and Mr. Ishii consulted back and forth for half a year, during which time our negotiations with the Public Works Department could not proceed. We then quietly waited for the development between the Public Works Department and the Japanese Consulate. Examining the Japanese methods of obstruction, the area of the extraterritorial roads in the Public Concession is mostly in the Northwest Two Districts, and the lives and property of the Japanese living in Shanghai are mostly based in the extraterritorial road section of the Northwest One District. They believe that after the area is returned to the jurisdiction of the Municipal Government, the protection of the Japanese will not be trusted. Therefore, they have tried their best to oppose the recovery. Later, because the Public Works Department was very eager to return the area to our side, the negotiations were quite promising, and the draft agreement was about to be finalized. Therefore, the Japanese Consul expressed to the Public Works Department that the Japanese side wanted to retain police power. However, this move concerns our national sovereignty, and the Public Works Department knew that it could not be accommodated by our side. Therefore, the two sides consulted on this point. The Japanese initially insisted on this proposal, and later demanded the establishment of a Japanese deputy police chief and the recruitment of Japanese special police officers. Discussions lasted for half a year. Because the Public Works Department and the Japanese Consulate kept strict secrets, there were few rumors outside. Even if there were rumors, they were not very detailed. Therefore, news about the recovery of the extraterritorial roads has been silent in the newspapers for more than half a year.

Recent Developments

It is heard that there have been new developments in the recent negotiations between the Public Works Department and the Japanese Consulate. Therefore, the Board of Directors of the Public Works Department once again brought up the old matter for discussion at the regular meeting last week. At the same time, there is news that the Public Works Department will continue with our side. Therefore, it has been confirmed that the Japanese Consulate has made concessions. However, the specific nature of this concession is still unclear because the two sides are still keeping secrets. Only the Public Works Department's statement that it will continue negotiations with our side has not been denied by any party.

Insufficient Japanese Cargo Ships Between Shanghai and Japan

Chinese Cargo Rejected

Japanese Self-Satisfaction

According to yesterday's Japanese-language Shanghai Daily News, the cargo ships of the Japanese Deng Chuan Shipping Company that travel between Japan and Shanghai, in addition to the designated route ships Dajia and Zhujun between Tokyo, there are also the Seiko and Mikasa between Osaka and Kobe. In the past, there were also the Kasagi and Yahata between Osaka and Kobe to receive and transport goods. Since the outbreak of the Manchurian Incident, the shipping industry has suddenly declined, and the transportation of goods has also suddenly decreased. Therefore, the number of cargo ships was also reduced by two. Today, the export of goods to Japan is very strong, and ships are insufficient. Commodities such as broad beans, rapeseed, cottonseed, pomace, bran, and beef bones are in large quantities. The outbound cargo of companies such as Mitsui, Yongfa, Yoshida, and Masuyuki in this port averages around 25,000 tons, but the capacity of the above two ships is only 3,600 tons, and they only travel back and forth twice a month. Therefore, transportation is quite difficult, and all parties hope to restore the previous ships to meet the demand. At the same time, the import of miscellaneous goods from Japan to this port is 1,500 to 2,000 tons per ship, and transportation is still insufficient.

Export Subsidy for Stored Silk Stopped Yesterday

More than 19,000 Bales Sold

The Reorganization and Promotion Associations End at the Same Time

The governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, in order to relieve the silk industry, issued a short-term public bond of 3 million yuan in the 21st year of the Republic (1932), and established the Stored Factory Silk Promotion and Stored Factory/Stored Cocoon Reorganization Committees to handle promotion and registration matters. For each bale of stored silk exported, the government subsidized 140 yuan of public bonds. The two committees were ordered to stop issuing subsidies at the end of May and stipulated a method for exceeding 20,000 bales. Yesterday was the deadline, and it is estimated that more than 19,000 bales have received government subsidies. This has been reported to the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Finance, and the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. As for the two committees being ordered to end, it has been decided that they will handle various unfinished procedures starting today.

Shanghai-Chengdu Line Inaugurated Today

New Aircraft for Shanghai-Guangdong Line to be Transported to Shanghai

The China National Aviation Corporation, in order to complete the Shanghai-Chengdu trunk line, sent the Bengbu aircraft piloted by Mr. Bender, head of the airline group, and pilot Mr. Allison to Chongqing for a test flight on the 28th of last month. The company spokesman claimed yesterday that the test flight of the Chongqing-Chengdu section was successful and the Shanghai-Chengdu line was scheduled to officially open at 8 am tomorrow (today). The one-way ticket from Shanghai to Chengdu is 100 yuan per person, and the round-trip ticket is 175 yuan per person. The postage for each flight zone (the Shanghai-Chengdu line has two flight zones) is 25 cents. It is also heard that the company's Shanghai-Guangdong line has been decided to have a test flight on July 1st, and the company has prepared all the equipment for each station along the line. Personnel are planned to be sent to arrange the work in separate groups. The aircraft used for the route has been ordered from the American Alliance Company for two aircraft, each costing more than 160,000 yuan. The aircraft can seat eight people and can travel more than 100 miles per hour. The aircraft can be transported in two weeks (New News Agency).

Unemployment Issue of Workers at Japanese-Owned Taishan Factory Resolved

Female Workers Transferred to Da Zhongyang Factory, Male Workers Dismissed

National News Agency reports that the Taishan Rubber Factory in Hongkou, owned by Japanese merchants, specializes in manufacturing Taishan rubber overshoes for sale in our country. After the September 18th Incident, Chinese people unanimously rejected Japanese goods, and the factory's business plummeted. It was then taken over by Huashangren Zhongyang Rubber Factory, which dispatched workers to continue working. The original 70-odd male and female workers of the factory were all unemployed and repeatedly requested the party and government authorities to provide relief. It is now learned that the case has been mediated by the Fourth District Rubber Industry Trade Union, which has reached an agreement with the Da Zhongyang Factory to allow all female workers to transfer to the factory for work, but all male workers will be given severance pay and dismissed. The workers have also expressed their agreement, and the dispute has been resolved.

Two Exchanges to Merge Today

Increase Capital Stock and Brokers

Inaugural Meeting to be Held in July

According to news from the Shanghai Chinese Securities Exchange, the Shanghai Chinese Securities Exchange and the Securities Department of the Shanghai Goods and Securities Exchange have resolved the merger issue according to the provisions of the Exchange Law and after three years of consultation on April 30th. It is scheduled to merge into the Shanghai Chinese Securities Exchange for business starting today. The original capital stock of the Shanghai Chinese Securities Exchange was 1 million yuan, and there were 55 brokers. It has now been decided that the Securities Department of the Goods Exchange will add 200,000 yuan of capital stock and 20 brokers. The Chinese side will also add 15 brokers, forming a new organization with a total capital stock of 1.2 million yuan and 80 brokers. An inaugural meeting will be held in July to elect officers.

Maritime Administration Bureau Stipulates Restrictions on Foreign Crew Members on Chinese Ships

Otherwise, Customs Will Not Allow Departure

National News Agency reports that the Shanghai Maritime Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Communications recently issued an order stipulating that Chinese crew members should be used as a principle for all Chinese ships. If it is necessary to hire foreign crew members, a certificate issued by the Ministry must be obtained, otherwise Customs may not allow the ship to depart. The Bureau has now ordered all shipping companies in the city to implement this regulation. As a result, companies such as Datong Renji Shipping Company and Haichang Shipping Company, where most of the shipmasters and first and second officers are Japanese, are deeply concerned that Customs will not allow them to travel on Shanghai, so they have dismissed all Japanese crew members and replaced them with Chinese crew members.

Businessmen and Residents of the North Sichuan Road War Zone Petitioned Party and Government Agencies Yesterday

Will Present to the Central Government for Request

North Sichuan Road and North Laobazi Road are located in the extraterritorial road areas. For decades, there has been no imposition of house tax. In the past, the Public Works Department compiled house numbers. In the 16th year of the Republic (1927), citizens demolished the blocked roads and blocked the main roads, automatically prying off the house numbers and re-nailing the Chinese house numbers. It is unknown that yesterday, Director Liang of the Tax Collection Office of the Zhabei Finance Bureau, disregarding the hardships of the merchants and residents, rashly sent two tax collectors, leading six policemen, to each shop to forcibly collect house tax, with great fanfare, threatening to arrest the employees. Therefore, at 3 pm, representatives of each shop gathered for a meeting and decided that more than 300 shops would jointly prepare a report and push Guan Qichuan, Jin Yongxiang, Wei Langxuan, Ye Qichang, and Hu Zhaoying to take the joint report to the Municipal Government to petition, requesting that the rights be recovered first and the house tax be collected later. Xu Shaoxiu was received, stated the intentions, and expressed his sympathy, promising to forward the above to the mayor to order the collection to stop. The representatives then said goodbye and went to the Municipal Party Headquarters, where Zhang Zhixiao, the representative, promised to forward it to the higher authorities for review. The representatives considered it satisfactory and withdrew. It is also heard that each shop has prepared another petition to the Central Party Headquarters and the Executive Yuan, requesting a ban.

The British-owned Four Seas Insurance Company at No. 17 on the Bund held its third annual shareholders' meeting the day before yesterday. All shareholders and directors attended, and Mr. Smith was publicly elected as chairman. In addition to reporting the purpose of the meeting and reading the business situation and various accounts of the previous year, the chairman made the following brief report: "Last year (1932), under the global economic downturn, various businesses showed no signs of recovery, and the Far East was no exception. Consequently, the insurance business also suffered a major blow. Fortunately, with the guidance of the board of directors and the efforts of the staff in various departments, the company was able to achieve special progress under this severe situation, which is gratifying for all shareholders. During this year, the effective insured amount increased from 202,480 taels to 2,513,280 taels. The total profit of various businesses was 104,819 taels, which is sufficient to demonstrate the company's business progress. The deposit of various reserves has also increased by more than double compared to the past, totaling 259,990.64 taels, which is even more sufficient to prove that the company's foundation is becoming increasingly solid. During this year, in addition to the Shanghai head office, branches were established in Hong Kong, Guangzhou, Peiping, Tianjin, and other places to operate various insurance businesses in these areas. In order to enhance the awareness of the Chinese people regarding the benefits of life insurance and to promote business development, the company, together with the responsible persons of various life insurance companies, established the Chinese Life Insurance Advancement Association, providing it with financial support to fulfill its mission of promoting the theories and benefits of life insurance and developing the Chinese life insurance industry, and writing various texts and books on life insurance science to educate the Chinese people about the understanding and investment of life insurance. In addition, the company's colleagues, considering the need for life insurance in China, in addition to the various policies already issued, plan to issue group insurance, industrial insurance, and other policies at low prices to meet the needs of the Chinese people. This is the general situation of the company in the past year. Although the company was established not long ago, its business situation has improved year by year, and future prospects are promising. It is not difficult to become the only financial institution in the Far East." After the chairman's report, the company continued to discuss various ongoing plans and passed the following resolutions: (1) The current surplus of 104,819 taels, together with the balance of 51,542.48 taels carried over from the previous year, after deducting the ordinary reserve of 140,187.51 taels to meet the requirement of 250,000 taels, the remaining balance of 16,171.97 taels will be carried over to the next year's calculation. Speelman, and A. J. Welchill as directors of the company. (5) Appoint Lowe, Bingham, and Matthewsill as auditors of the company. After the various resolutions were passed, a gathering was held and then adjourned.

Debate on Li Guojie Case Concluded

Public and Private Lawsuits Both Concluded, Sentencing on June 5th

Lawyers on Both Sides Eloquently Debated for Two Hours

Westerner Sutterly Called as Witness

Li Guojie, the former general manager of the China Merchants Bureau, was originally sentenced to three years in prison by the Shanghai District Court for allegedly breaching trust, harming the interests of the bureau, committing fraud in borrowing foreign debts, and bribing Supervisor Chen Fumu with 700,000 taels. Li refused to accept the sentence and appealed. The Criminal Division 1 of the Jiangsu High Court, with Presiding Judge Lin Zhechang, Judges Fang Wen and Si Wen, Prosecutor Hong Guifen, Clerks Qian Zemin and Li Wang, and others, came to Shanghai to hear the case in the District Court. Yesterday afternoon at 1 p.m., the trial continued in the first courtroom. The head of the China Business Company was summoned.

Sutterly testified that he was 73 years old and an American. He knew Li Guojie. (Question) Did Li Guojie, as manager of the China Merchants Bureau, sign a contract with the China Business Company? (Answer) Yes. (Question) Was it for borrowing money for docks, building storage, and buying ships? (Answer) Yes. (Question) How much money was borrowed? (Answer) 3,000 taels. (Question) What was the interest rate? (Answer) 9% per week. (Question) Was there a commission? (Answer) Usually 2.5%. This loan was for issuing bonds, and the actual receipt was 85%, which is different from ordinary loans. It's like the city's bonds being sold at 80% of their face value. However, it would take ten years to repay the full face value. However, this loan plan was very large, and as soon as a floor was built, the China Merchants Bureau could develop on this land. As for the harsh conditions, this is the usual practice in Shanghai, the same for everyone, so that they know the restrictions. Moreover, the China Merchants Bureau couldn't even pay for the two Norwegian ships it bought, and tried to evade payment, so we had to set up retention rights, etc., to wait for payment. (Question) Did it also infringe on ownership? (Answer) Bonds, that is, issuing bonds for ships, must have the ships as collateral, so there is ownership. (Question) When were the bonds issued? (Answer) Early September. (Question) Was there an advance payment? (Answer) 700,000 taels. (Question) What was it for? (Answer) Checks. (Question) Who told you about it? (Answer) Li Guojie said that according to us, it was to fulfill the debt payment, but they wanted to borrow 700,000 first, and said it again and again, so they paid 700,000. (Question) Did you know it was paid to Chen Fumu? (Answer) I paid the money to the China Merchants Bureau, and handed over the bank certificates to us, so that we could redeem them in the future. We took the receipt from the China Merchants Bureau. (Question) Did Li Guojie say that there would be a contract after the payment? (Answer) No. If there were such words, we wouldn't allow him to come. (Question) Who delivered the 700,000 taels? (Answer) Comprador Dou Yaoting. (Question) What did you say when you handed it to Dou? (Answer) I told him to send it to the China Merchants Bureau. (Question) Did Dou say anything? (Answer) He didn't say anything, just handed me a package. (Question) How did you deliver the 710,000 taels? (Answer) With checks. (Question) Was there any cash? (Answer) No. (Question) Was there a commission in the 1.5 million taels? (Answer) Absolutely none. (Question) Was the 2.5% commission shared? 0 (Answer) No, we believed that Mr. Li was cautious and never defaulted on a penny. Later, Nanjing telegraphed me, and I went to Nanjing to see Minister Song, only to learn about this matter, and immediately explained the situation, how I didn't like it, and that it could be resolved. Now we are sincerely negotiating, etc. At this point, the official (questioned)

Li Guojie: What about Sutterly's testimony? (Answer) Just that he is older and confused 20 million with 30 million. The prosecutor Zhan Guifen then gave his opinion, believing that Li was guilty, but that the legal provisions had to be changed, etc. Then, the defense lawyers Zhang Yipeng, Sha Xunyi, Jiang Yiping, etc. gave their arguments on the legal facts, which lasted for about two hours. The questioning official then declared the conclusion of the public prosecution debate, and the sentencing was set for 11 a.m. on June 5. Then, he began to interrogate the attached civil lawsuit. Liu Hongsheng, the legal representative of the China Merchants Bureau, appointed lawyer Wang Youling as his agent, stating that regardless of whether there was a criminal offense, the 700,000 taels was taken by Li Guojie, and there was no proof of whether it was handed over. According to the provisions of the Civil Code, he requested a judgment ordering the return of the money, and requested a provisional execution to seize private property, etc. The official questioned Li, who refused to compensate, and said that the money was taken by Chen Fumu and had nothing to do with him. His defense lawyers also stated that the government sent a supervisor to restrict Li's exercise of his duties, and the supervisor was the manager, while the manager was like an employee and could not be held responsible. They also compared various matters, such as the case in the twelfth year of the Republic of China, where the head of the trial court, Mei Yigu, absconded with the money, and the receiving and dispatching clerks and accountants who did not transfer the money were sentenced to pay compensation, and refuted that the China Merchants Bureau was not an ordinary store, etc. At this point, the lawyers on both sides had a great debate. The official again declared the conclusion of the private lawsuit debate, and also set the sentencing for June 5 at the same time, and then adjourned the court.

Continuous All-Out Brawl on the Samsung Stage

Zhao Ruquan First Performed Twenty Episodes of the Peng Gong Case

General Audience Continued to Fight Each Other

[A Disturbance After Zhao Ruquan Was Detained]

Zhao Ruquan, a famous actor on the Samsung stage, was in charge of the backstage manager of the stage. Zhou Bingchen was the front-stage manager, and each was originally responsible for their own duties. However, Zhao and Zhou had deep differences and could not cooperate, and were mutually exclusive. Recently, Zhou reported to the Laozha Police Station that Zhao had embezzled more than 30,000 gold coins of public funds. However, after investigation, only 1,240 yuan of embezzlement was found. The police station transferred the case to the First Special District District Court to issue an arrest warrant. On the night of the 29th, detectives Chen Yonggui and Yang Guanying rushed to the Samsung Stage Theater on Niuzhuang Road to arrest him. Zhao was playing Ouyang De in the twenty episodes of the Peng Gong Case drama, showing his skills on stage. When Chen and Yang arrested him, the audience suddenly saw Ouyang De being taken away by the officials, and there was a great uproar. Although the play ended, the audience did not leave. Because they had spent money but had not seen the whole picture, they demanded refunds. The director of the stage said that the play had ended and the customers had not suffered any losses, and refused to refund the tickets. This aroused public anger, and an all-out brawl broke out again. Teapots and teacups flew around, and chairs and stools were destroyed and thrown. For a time, the order was chaotic. The Laozha Police Station was notified and immediately ordered a large team of armed detectives to suppress the disturbance, and arrested Lu Huiquan and Hu Shoufu on the spot. The rest scattered and fled. The next morning, the police station sent Zhao Ruquan, Lu, and Hu to the First Special District Court. Presiding Judge Feng Shide interrogated them. Lawyer Ru Baoyi of the police station explained the case. Then, Zhou Bingchen, the plaintiff, appointed lawyers Chen Tingrui and Yuan Yang'an to appear in court to defend him. Zhao Ruquan, the defendant, also appointed lawyer Jiang Yiping to briefly defend him. After the presiding judge Feng ruled that the defendant Zhao Ruquan should be remanded in custody and rescheduled for a hearing on Saturday. As for the two defendants Lu and Hu, who were accused of destroying the stage, Judge Wang Ren heard the case. Lawyer Jiang Baolian of the police station stated that the stage suffered a loss of about 1,000 yuan. When questioned, the defendants shirked their responsibilities. Judge Wang ruled that each should be fined 50 yuan as a warning.

Co-Tenant Suddenly Turns Thief

Gangs Up with Bandits Under the Guise of Mahjong

Howls Upstairs in the Middle of the Night to Commit Robbery

No. 22 Jubao Lane, Chengdu Road, is a one-story building with four households. The sub-landlord is Huang Weimin, who lives in the front building and rents out the pavilion to He Changbao from Zhenjiang. He used to be a battalion commander under Xing Shilian, but resigned to recuperate in Shanghai due to a foot injury. The back of the lobby downstairs is rented to Mo Baosheng, and the back building is rented to a Chen family. All was peaceful. Unexpectedly, Mo Baosheng was actually a member of a gang. Although his usual behavior was illegal, the co-tenants were unaware of the details. On the night of May 25, he gathered six accomplices and went to his home to play. After 10 p.m., they became interested in gambling. Mo invited He Changbao and two of his accomplices to play mahjong, while the other four watched. By the time the twelve rounds ended, it was already 3 a.m. All the co-tenants had fallen asleep. Seeing that the time had come, Mo let out a yell to notify his accomplices. They each took out pistols, warning everyone not to make a sound. They first tied He with ropes and kept him under surveillance in the back room. Then they went upstairs and entered He's bedroom. He's wife, Chen, and daughter, Chunxiang (16 years old), were awakened from their sleep. They were ordered not to make a sound, forced to hand over the key, and robbed of a gold bracelet, a gold chain, a gold sheet, as well as 80 yuan in cash, clothes, and other items, estimated to be worth 751 yuan. They took the stolen goods and escaped with Mo's wife. Later, He's wife managed to untie her husband's ropes and reported to the Xinzha Police Station. Detectives Tao Rubing and Sun Jishan were dispatched to investigate and brought back a mahjong set and a rope to the police station. Because a similar case had occurred on Ma Huo Road a few days ago, a strict investigation was started. He Changbao's daughter, He Chunxiang, was taken to various public places, tea houses, and hotels to investigate. It wasn't until 9:40 a.m. the day before yesterday that Zhou Shaoqing, a thief from Changzhou, was found in the Liyuan Tea House in the City God Temple in the city. He's daughter identified Zhou as the thief who had held a gun and robbed them at the time. He was arrested by the Zhengan Bureau police and taken back to the police station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Criminal Division 8 of the First Special District Court. Lawyer Li Zhishan of the police station detailed the circumstances of the case and requested a postponement to apprehend the accomplices. He Changbao, along with his wife Chen and daughter Chunxiang, testified that they were robbed by Mo Baosheng, a co-tenant, under the pretext of playing mahjong. The defendant who was arrested was indeed a thief holding a gun. Defendant Zhou Shaoqing confessed that he had visited Mo's house once in February, which allowed him to meet He, but that he neither gambled nor robbed that night. Please investigate. Judge Wu Tingqi verified the confession and ordered Zhou to be remanded in custody for seven days for further investigation.

Cotton Cloth Industry Raises Prices

Increased Taxation After the Implementation of the New Tax

Due to the increase in cotton cloth taxation after the promulgation of the new tax rules, the Shanghai Cotton Cloth Industry Association believed that this would have a significant impact on the future of the business. It convened a joint meeting of directors and supervisors to resolve that the price of cotton cloth would be increased immediately to supplement the costs. The association's letter to various cotton cloth shops is recorded as follows: Notice is hereby given that the tax rules promulgated on May 22 have greatly increased the taxation on cotton cloth. All of us in the industry, in order to protect our capital and business interests, should increase the price of goods to supplement the costs. After convening a meeting of the industry and submitting it to the eleventh joint meeting of the directors and supervisors, it was resolved to notify all members of the industry to increase the price of goods immediately. Corresponding records can be reported and it is hoped that you will follow the procedure and not pursue short-term gains and divide each other.

Jiangsu Maritime Patrol Team Forcibly Collects Flag Fee from Fishing Boats

Shanghai Fisheries Association Telegraphs to Stop It

Zhu Songzhou, the captain of the Jiangsu Maritime Patrol Team of the Yangtze River Provincial Water Police General Bureau, has several patrol ships stationed in places such as Maji, Shengshan, and Sijiao in Jiangsu in order to forcibly collect fishing protection fees. Under the guise of protecting and arresting, he forcibly collects fishing protection flag fees of 30 to 50 yuan from fishing boats passing by. Those who are unable to pay are arrested, beaten, arbitrarily imprisoned, and their boxes and chests are turned over, acting like bandits. They extort and defraud in all sorts of ingenious ways. More than 2,000 fishing boats have been harmed, and more than 70,000 yuan in fishing flag fees have been collected. The fishermen are heartbroken, cry out in pain, and have repeatedly requested the Shanghai Fisheries Association for relief. The City Fisheries Association has telegraphed the authorities to stop it quickly. The original telegrams are recorded on the left.

Telegram to the Director of the Water Police Bureau

Jiang Junjian, Director of the Yangtze River Provincial Water Police General Bureau in Hankou, Zhu Songzhou, the captain of the Jiangsu Maritime Guerrilla Team, which is directly under your bureau and stationed on the islands of Maji, Hujiao, and Shengshan, which belong to Chongming County, has abused his power to issue fishing boat flag permits and forcibly collect permit fees of 30 to 50 yuan per boat. If the fishermen are unable to pay, they are beaten. At a time when the fishing industry is in extreme decline, it is impossible to bear this burden. In addition to submitting the flag permit separately, I respectfully request that you stop it immediately to relieve the people of Jiangsu from their plight.

Telegram to Chairman Jiang

Jiang, Chairman of the Military Commission of Nanjing, and Chen, Minister of Industry, Chongming County belongs to Maji Sijiao Shengshan and other islands, stationed in the Yangtze River Provincial Water Police General Bureau directly under the Jiangsu Maritime Patrol Team Captain Zhu Songzhou abuse issued fishing boat flag inspection, and forcibly collect the fee, each boat thirty yuan, the fishermen and other set powerless payment, that is, beaten, at this time the fishing industry is extremely depressed, it is impossible to bear this extra burden, in addition to submitting the flag separately, I respectfully request that you immediately transfer the telegram to stop it, to the Su people, urgent to be fate.

After the Robbery of the Taizhou Ship, the Shipping Association Telegraphs to Urge Strict Apprehension

Wenling and Huangyan Water Police Pursue and Fight Fiercely with Pirates

A Small Headman Captured, Two Water Police Killed

After the Taihou-Shanghai line of the Taihou Steamship, owned by Lian'an Navigation Company, was robbed on the 24th of last month, the Wenling and Huangyan water police jointly pursued the pirates and a fierce battle broke out. The details are as follows:

Fierce Battle Erupted

According to a reporter from Xinsheng News Agency, the Lian'an Company announced yesterday that two water police officers were killed and four passengers and teahouse staff were injured, and one passenger was kidnapped in the robbery of the Taizhou ship. The Haiment Taizhou Steamship Head Office immediately telegraphed to strictly apprehend the pirates and rescue the kidnapped passengers. The Second Brigade of the Water Police stationed at Jinqing Port in Huangyan and the Wenling Water Police Bureau immediately dispatched armed water police to jointly pursue the pirates. On the evening of the 26th, a fierce battle broke out with the pirates in the pirate den east of Jinqing Port. A small headman of the pirates, Lin Erdi, was captured alive and sent to the headquarters for strict punishment. Several pirates were killed and three guns were seized. Two water police officers, Huang Zhengqi and Li Chang'an, were killed.

Sailing to Shanghai Tomorrow

As for whether the kidnapped passenger Jin Ziqing has been rescued, the Haiment Head Office report did not mention it. Details will be available when the Dahua ship arrives in Shanghai on June 1. However, the Taizhou ship is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 2nd. The notice is recorded as follows: The Taizhou ship is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on June 2 and sail to Dingpu, Shipu, and Haiment on the 3rd. It will continue to operate as usual afterwards. For fear that it has not been fully informed, this notice is given.

Telegraphic Request for Strict Apprehension

The Shanghai Shipping Industry Association sent a fast mail telegram to the Zhejiang Provincial Government in Hangzhou, the Zhejiang Provincial Security Department, the Zhenhai Zhejiang Offshore Water Police Bureau, and the Shanghai Maritime Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, stating that the member Taizhou Xinji Shipping Company stated in a letter that the company's Taizhou ship sailed from Haiment to Shanghai on the 24th of this month and arrived at the waters of Nanbei and Bamen. Suddenly, pirates disguised as passengers opened fire and robbed the ship. Two water police officers and a girl on board were killed, and a tea attendant and two water police officers were injured. One passenger was kidnapped. The robbery lasted about 23 hours, and dozens of searches were carried out. The silver dollars and ship documents stored in the ship's accounting room, as well as the silver dollars, clothing, luggage, etc. carried by the crew and passengers, were all looted. Finally, they were forced to sail to Langqishan to land and escape. In addition to the company in Haiment dividing the Zhejiang Offshore Water Police Bureau, the Zhejiang Provincial Government, and the military and police agencies stationed in Haiment to strictly apprehend and encircle the bandits, it is appropriate to write to the association to forward the letter to the Shanghai Maritime Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Communications for the record, and to send it to the military and police agencies in Zhejiang to strictly investigate and deal with it, so as to pacify the bandits and ensure the safety of travelers. The Shanghai Shipping Industry Association Chairman Yu Hede knocked into the trap.

A Local Thug Claiming to Be a Communist Stabs a Police Officer

Shan Wen, a police officer from the Third District of Pudong, was stationed at the intersection of the new Lan Ni Du street around 10:30 PM on the 29th. At that moment, a middle-aged man reported to him that communist bandits were secretly meeting in the back street and requested an arrest. The officer, considering the matter of sedition, followed him to investigate. Unexpectedly, upon reaching a dark area near the Li family residence on the north side, the youth pulled out a sharp blade, proclaiming himself a member of the Communist Party. He then stabbed the officer violently in the back, penetrating deeply, and fled the scene. The wounded officer collapsed unconscious. A passerby discovered him and urgently reported it to the neighboring station. The injured officer was carried to Pudong Hospital for treatment, leaving a trail of blood. After being rescued and awakened by the doctor, the wound was cleaned and bandaged. District Chief Zhang Wuqin, upon receiving the report, immediately instructed the police to apprehend the culprit. He also telegraphed each precinct and team to cooperate in the capture. By midnight, Police Chief Guo Yongliang had arrested a suspect, the culprit's aunt, Ms. Dai, at No. 20, Lane 162, the site of the incident, and brought her to the district for questioning. She claimed her nephew, Ling Houlang, suffered from mental illness. Moments later, the suspect's uncle, Lu Chuanlin, also arrived at the district to report, volunteering to assist in the arrest of his nephew. By 7:00 AM the next morning (the 30th), Chuanlin arrived at the Dada Wharf in Nanshi, where he spotted the suspect preparing to flee back to his native Chongming. He immediately reported it to the wharf police, who apprehended him and brought him to the First District. Subsequently, Police Chief Guo from the Third District transferred him back for interrogation by District Chief Zhang. The suspect confessed that he was 31 years old and from Chongming, working as a mate on an iron barge at No. 156, Huide Li. He claimed that the previous night he had a dream where his cousin (the son of his uncle) forcibly violated his wife. The next morning, he questioned his uncle, but was scolded for being unreasonable. Therefore, the previous night, he took a knife intending to kill his uncle to relieve his anger. Suddenly, he saw a police officer walking towards him with a gun, assuming it was his uncle who had reported him. As a preemptive measure, he wounded the officer. The District Chief found his confession quite absurd, as if he were truly mentally ill. He was to be charged with assaulting a public security police officer and sent to the General Bureau for interrogation. During the escort, the suspect murmured incoherently, declaring that he had joined the Communist Party and was very happy, while also displaying a bitter smile, which was quite pathetic. As for the injured officer, his injuries were severe, and he had been transferred to Shanghai Hospital in Nanshi for medical treatment.

Zhao Shaojing Overwhelmed with Emotions on the Dragon Boat Festival, Drowns Himself in the Huangpu River

A Heartbreaking Suicide Note · A Pitiful Situation

| Luckily Rescued by a Boatman and Saved from Death |

Yesterday at 2:30 PM, a middle-aged man boarded the No. 9 ferry at the Chunjiang Wharf in Pudong and crossed to the center of the river. He suddenly jumped into the river to commit suicide. Captain Dai Lanfang managed to rescue him and sent him to the Customs Water Police Station. He identified himself as Zhao Shaojing, styled Pihua, 30 years old, from Jiangbei, residing at his mother-in-law's house in Zhujiaqiao, Jiangwan. He used to work at the Shunyu Money Shop on Tiantong Road in Hongkou, which has since closed down. He had been unemployed for three years and had experienced the hardship of economic pressure. He had also been looked down upon by relatives and friends. Therefore, before the Dragon Boat Festival, he left home and stayed at a small inn in the Caishi Street area. He had attempted suicide by swallowing opium, but it was ineffective. On the Dragon Boat Festival, seeing families gathering happily, he was overcome with emotions. He secretly wrote two suicide notes and waited until today to resolve to drown himself. Two letters were found on his person, one to his father and one to his wife. The detective chief instructed Bao Tan Yao Guofa to summon his family to the station and allow them to take him home. The letter to his wife is transcribed below: "To my beloved wife Qin: What day is today? A day when families gather to celebrate the Dragon Boat Festival, but also the day when we, husband and wife, are forever separated. The thought of suicide has been with me for many days. I tried swallowing raw opium the other day, but it didn't work. I suppose I'm not meant to die by fire, but by water. How sad! Every day I live, you suffer another day. People live to be a hundred, but must eventually die. I'm not afraid to die early, and it's better for you to start planning for your future. I hope you will send our child to be raised by my mother and remarry as soon as possible to find happiness. I'm always sorry to you. Your foolish husband, Zhao Yu."

Sixty-Third Time

Reader's Advisory

Seeking Education and Joining the Army

丨Letter from Mr. Zhou Min'an of Shaoxing丨

Dear Editor,

I am a young man who has lost the opportunity to study due to economic pressures and environmental constraints! I graduated from elementary school two years ago, and I really wanted to go to middle school, but I couldn't! My family is so poor that they can't even make a living, so how can they afford to send me to school? After graduation, I didn't have a proper job, so I wandered around every day, wasting my precious time in the word "wandering." My mother is a thoughtful person, and she thought that if I kept playing like this, I would only be consuming and not earning. So, she ordered me to go to the mountains near our home to collect firewood, or to help others, even if it was just to get a meal or a dime. But my education was neglected! Sometimes, I would try to steal some time from my work to study, but my mother would scold me, saying that I was lazy and that reading books was useless. Sadly, I had to put down my books and do other things. Sometimes, I would go to the mountains to chop wood, secretly hiding a few textbooks that I had already read under the firewood basket. After chopping the wood, I would sit on the mountain and read. I would only stop when it was getting dark. This continued until last autumn. Later, someone recommended me to work as an apprentice in a small pharmacy in Shanghai. However, the store closed down due to losses, and I lost my job and returned home. Now? I can only steal some time from my work to read your newspaper every day (for the shortest period of time). (Because when I was in school, the school also subscribed to your newspaper. After class, I considered your newspaper my only companion. Since the September 18th Incident two years ago, I have been sharing a subscription to your newspaper with others.) The rest of the time, I work as a laborer to solve the problem of food. But my desire to study has not died. Sometimes, when I see the recruitment advertisements of various schools in the newspaper, I almost cry! And I stare enviously at those纨绔 children who go from elementary school to middle school! I am so envious! Sometimes, I think to myself: They are human beings, and I am a human being, and we live in the same society. How can they have the blessing of receiving education? Alas! Why can't I even afford a correspondence school (such as the Kaiming Correspondence Middle School and others)? Even if I want to study on my own, Heaven doesn't give me enough time, and I don't have the ability to buy ordinary self-study reference books. Besides the textbooks I read before and old novels such as Romance of the Eastern and Western Han Dynasties, Xue Rengui Conquers the East, Seven Heroes and Five Gallants, and Biography of the Loyal Martyrs, there is nothing else in my home! Sir, in my situation, what methods can I use to study?

Also, I think that if I really don't have the opportunity to study, then I am the most pitiful person in the world! What is the point of living? I might as well commit suicide. However, now that the country is in crisis, it is better to join the army than to commit suicide! Moreover, the enemy has already invaded our Hebei, and Peiping and Tianjin are in danger. Joining the army and going north to die for the country is more valuable than committing suicide! Sir, do you think joining the army is okay? Please use your vast talent and rich experience to solve these two problems for me in your column.

Reply will be published tomorrow.

Recently, Mr. He Ju of Shaoxing wrote a letter, saying that he had spent several years and countless efforts to invent a kind of thermos bottle based on scientific principles, which can keep heat for ten days and keep cold for one month, and its effect is far better than any thermos bottle sold on the market. However, due to lack of capital, he cannot set up a factory to manufacture it by himself. He intends to seek cooperation from domestic industrialists or sell the invention rights. He asked this newspaper to introduce it on his behalf. This newspaper believes that it is a pity if Mr. He's invention is not made known to the world, so it is happy to publish the introduction as above. If domestic industrialists are interested in this, they can directly contact Mr. He in Dongguan, Shaoxing.

Domestic Goods Forum

The Year of Domestic Goods at a Critical Juncture

— Yang Yun

Since our National Government implemented the new tariff law on May 22 and raised tariff rates, the most vocal opponents have been Japanese merchants, especially those in the cotton cloth business. They have been holding meetings with Japanese merchants in various ports for days to study countermeasures, even falsely accusing it of being a disguised method of boycotting Japanese goods, believing that Japanese goods have no room for expansion in the world market and that China is the only way out, which must not be let go. They have proposed eight resolutions to protest to our government, stating that if these tariff rates are not revised, not only will cotton yarn merchants be hit, but all Japanese industrial and commercial enterprises in China will be affected, and as a result, Japan's trade with China will decline from now on. This problem is more serious than the Shanghai Incident of last year, and if it is not resolved properly, terrible incidents may occur. At the same time, they are calling on the Japanese government and the Japan Cotton Yarn and Cloth Exporters Association and the Osaka Cotton Cloth Merchants Association to provide the same assistance. The Japanese, who are accustomed to doing business with guns, clearly know that China has the sovereign right to tariff independence and has no legal basis for protest. They insist on using force to intimidate and seek improper solutions, holding meetings here and negotiating there, making unreasonable demands and expanding their unwarranted movement. Minister Yoshizawa has lodged a protest with me, stating that "Your country's increase in tariffs has greatly impacted Japanese trade and harmed Sino-Japanese friendly relations, which is regrettable and respectfully requests reconsideration." Japan's representative to the World Economic Conference, Ishii, pointed out that China's boycott is the biggest obstacle to commerce and will propose a response plan at the Economic Conference. The Japanese, from top to bottom, have long regarded our country as nothing and have nothing to fear, except for this boycott issue. There are no Chinese merchants for Japanese merchants, and the benefit of Japanese goods is the harm of domestic goods. At this critical juncture, why are our domestic goods merchants indifferent and unmoved, allowing the Japanese to use their ghostly tricks to destroy the dying vitality of our domestic goods? If you don't believe me, please tell me about the recent false accusations against domestic goods merchants. On the 24th of this month, a Shanghai newspaper published a headline saying "A Certain Society, the Source of the Shanghai Incident, Suddenly Purchased Japanese Yarn, and the Boycott of Japanese Goods Is Gradually Coming to an End," which stated that "Huang Fu entered Beiping and the ceasefire agreement is about to be established, and the boycott of Japanese goods is also easing, and the future is promising. Since the Manchurian Incident, the Tianjin Gang, the Qingdao Gang, and the Qinhuangdao Gang, as well as the Shanghai business community, are still in the midst of boycotting goods, but recently, they have gradually started purchasing Japanese yarn and cloth. What is most noteworthy is that a certain society with the strongest Kuomintang color and the direct cause of the Shanghai Incident has also been rumored to have purchased Japanese yarn. If the leader of this boycott has flattered Japanese yarn, then the Shanghai boycott movement seems to be coming to an end." The Japanese clearly know that a certain society has its own yarn factory in Hangzhou, spinning and weaving by itself, without the need to seek outside help, so they do not hesitate to create this absurd and unfounded rumor. Their purpose is (1) to seduce the public and deceive ignorant Chinese merchants, so as to strengthen their psychology of purchasing Japanese goods, thinking that the leader of the boycott has no courage to boycott, then the other factories and shops can purchase them. (2) The cotton cloth industry has been the hardest hit by Japanese commercial attacks in China. Tracing back to the beginning, since a certain society was founded in the early years of the Republic of China, cotton cloth factories have sprung up like mushrooms, enough to boycott Japanese goods invisibly, which is most hated by the Japanese. Therefore, they say "the strongest Kuomintang color" and "the leader of the boycott," doing their best to slander and exclude them, and their fierce and vicious purpose is to put our domestic goods merchants to death. Regular troops and surprise troops are advancing simultaneously, but our domestic goods merchants, except for the society itself negotiating with the newspaper, are indifferent and let the Japanese use their tricks without any assistance or expression? I believe that today's domestic goods merchants should make the greatest determination, stand firm and clear the fields, and strictly implement the following measures to save themselves and the country.

(1) Unanimously support the new tariffs and express to the government that the autonomy of tariffs must not be compromised in the slightest.

(2) Automatically organize inspection agencies and report each other to prevent Japanese goods from being smuggled in to damage the development of domestic goods. Nor should the Japanese be allowed to make false accusations to slander pure domestic goods merchants.

(3) Pay attention to mail delivery. It is heard that recently Japanese goods have invaded the interior, mostly by mail, and it is heard that they are delivered from places such as Nanxiang, and many foreign commercial ships along the Yangtze River have their own postal services. This kind of transportation is countless.

(4) Alas, the anti-Japanese war is powerless, and the agreement is about to be concluded. The fate of the country is at this point, and the whole country is heartbroken. If my domestic goods merchants do not have this determination and let the Japanese scold us as Chinese merchants who are blinded by greed (as the Daily News says), then the life of the domestic goods industry will end in this Year of Domestic Goods. This is truly a cause for weeping and sighing.

Talks on Domestic Goods

Stability

— Ke Ding'an

The word "stability" originally came from Buddhism. Its meaning is to first have specialized thought and then hold on to a firm determination. This is called "stability." People in the new era who read these words of mine will say that I am outdated. Then, of course, I will not admit it, because, to put it more broadly, from national affairs to family trifles, there is a great truth between these two words "stability." The current political chaos, diplomatic humiliation, and family disputes are all due to the lack of stability of those who bear great responsibility.

If we have a firm will to carry out something, although it may not be successful immediately, but with such a determination, even if there are some setbacks in the middle, future success is certain. If you feel disheartened when you encounter a slight setback, thinking that "the future is bleak and there is no hope," and even stop halfway, then your disappointment will be ten thousand times more painful than if you had not carried out something.

We don't need to talk about national affairs. What I want to talk about now is the greatest responsibility at the moment, which is the issue of domestic goods. I fundamentally oppose the saying "Chinese people should promote Chinese goods." You would think that people of a country should naturally purchase products from their own country to prevent money from flowing out. This is a matter of course, but in China, you cannot say this. Since the opening of the sea ban, foreign goods have been shipped to China in thousands of boxes. Curious Chinese people have flocked to them, accumulating a long history of nearly a hundred years, which has created the current situation: "Foreign goods sell well, domestic goods are sluggish." Ordinary domestic goods manufacturers and enthusiastic patriots compete to chant the slogan of "promoting domestic goods." I remember in 1915, after the Japanese forced Yuan Shikai to sign the Twenty-One Demands, I also formed a patriotic ten-person group with my friends, promoting the boycott of enemy goods. At that time, I fundamentally opposed the word "promote" in "promoting domestic goods." It would be more accurate to say "practical use" rather than "promote," because "promote" is an abstract noun. Whether you promote it or not, when it comes to "practical use," you must use it practically. It seems to be more accurate than promotion.

Let's talk about the word "stability" again. In the late Qing Dynasty, wasn't the Anchor brand towel very popular in the market? In the early years of the Republic of China, the XX Industrial Company in Shanghai, seeing that their towels were selling so well in the market, implemented a boycott and produced a towel with better material than the Anchor brand to boycott it. Sure enough, in less than a year, Anchor products were greatly affected and eventually became unsustainable and disappeared. Anchor also had a Double Cats brand of matches, which also went crazy in the Chinese market. Later, the Chinese XX factory produced goods to boycott it, and it suffered the same fate as the Anchor brand towels. Just looking at these two daily necessities, are there still traces of Anchor goods in the Chinese market today? I think no matter what, they will not be found again.

Why do the towels of the Chinese XX Industrial Company and the matches of the XX factory have such amazing miracles? In the end, there is nothing else, just the benefits of implementing based on "stability."

You should know that the success of a cause is not simple. Zeng Wenzheng Gong said: "Don't ask about future harvests, but ask about current cultivation." Harvest is a future matter that cannot be seen; cultivation is a present matter. Whether you are diligent or not, whether you are patient or not. If you do it based on stability, without the slightest懈怠, you will always achieve the goal of success.

Since "stability" is so important for producers, can we consumers be casual and without stability at all? No, no, consumers need "stability" as much as producers. If you buy casually, isn't that a big obstacle for producers? General consumers! First, recognize "our era"! Second, take on "our responsibility"! Finally, connect them together and complete them in one breath, and everyone "actually use domestic goods"! From today onwards, keep doing this in a practical way, and never look back. Because one glance will make you lose all your previous efforts. From the 4th year of the Republic of China to now, there have been many excellent examples. The effect of this fact is all based on the word "stability."

The Laborer and the Capitalist

— Zhang Mengzhao

Now: Everyone knows that silk factories have been defeated miserably. However: There are the most laborers. The largest-scale yarn factory. It is also being stirred up by evil merchants acting as accomplices, the demon of dumping into the Chinese mainland 丨Japanese yarn丨. Coupled with the government's failure to promptly implement dumping taxes, reduce unified tax rates and freight rates, and encourage cotton planting, the yarn factory is finally forced to reduce work and move towards decline. The lives of hundreds of thousands of laborers are gradually hanging upside down! Alas! In the eventful month of May, we hope that laborers will stand on the same front as capitalists, work hard, and create a bright path. Capitalists are painstakingly planning to maintain your lives. If labor and capital can work together to resist foreign aggression, and be as strong as steel and cement, then the Chinese market belongs to China, and laborers are the basic force of domestic goods. In the future, when foreign goods are defeated, laborers will be especially meritorious and worthy of everyone's praise.

The Problem of Reducing Work in Yarn Factories

— Qiu Guangting

Laborers are employed by factories to engage in production; factories are places where laborers exchange labor for money to support their lives. Factories rely on the strength of laborers to complete their production, and laborers rely on the gains from factory production to supply their lives. If laborers do not exert their ability to engage in production, the production volume will be thin, and the price of finished products will be high, making them incomparable to factories with superior production, and the business will tend to decline. If you want production to advance to superior, you must employ more laborers. When the number of laborers increases, and the wages per piece of finished product are fixed, the wages per person must decrease due to the increase in the total number of people. If wages are low, it is difficult for laborers to have a good life individually. If factories need to maintain a minimum standard of living for individuals, they must provide considerable wages. The total cost of wages always exceeds the standard wage per piece and is more than those with fewer people and higher wages. Since the rationalization of work was advocated in various advanced industrial countries, everyone has been striving to reduce consumption and increase production. They have simplified complex projects so that they can maximize production with the least amount of effort, and they have eliminated wasteful consumption to reduce power and manpower. To the extreme, the need for labor has been reduced, and the number of laborers needed has also decreased. Old factories want to keep pace with them to avoid being eliminated, so there has been a recent trend of laying off workers. However, the standard of living has been advancing over the years, and if wages do not increase, laborers cannot have a good life. If wages increase and the number of people does not decrease, the increase in wages will increase the number of people, and the finished products will inevitably be difficult to sell due to increased consumption, which is also a burden that factories cannot bear. To seek both, the only way is to give full play to the ability of laborers, reduce the number of people, laborers can exert their ability to achieve the success of both people with the strength of one person, factories give high wages, encourage their ability, laborers may be happy in their work because of the possibility, factories can also reduce the number of people and reduce the payment of wages.

Taking textile factories as an example, there are more than 4 million spindles in the country, of which 2.4 million spindles are operated by Chinese people themselves, and 1.8 million spindles are operated by Japanese people. I believe that the imperfect tax system is not enough to protect factories operated by Chinese people themselves, causing them to prosper. The imperfect social organization cannot maintain each other, causing the spinning industry to develop. Political instability and fluctuating public sentiment are all direct and indirect reasons why the textile industry cannot be promoted. The large number of laborers and the large payment of wages violate the principles of rationalization of production and cannot be compared with Japanese factories in China. From cleaning cotton to fine spinning, Japanese factories require an average of 140 laborers per 10,000 spindles, while Chinese factories in Shanghai require 220 laborers. Counting the work of shaking yarn and maintenance, Japanese factories require about 250 people, and Chinese factories in Shanghai require about 310 people. A certain factory in Nantong requires more than 800 laborers per 10,000 spindles on average. Recently, due to the collapse of the rural economy and weak purchasing power, coupled with the dumping of Japanese goods, the inventory of each factory has been huge. The Chinese Cotton Yarn Factory Association has resolved to reduce work to reduce inventory and to reorganize internally, reduce excessive consumption, and reduce costs, so as not to be exploited by their dumping policy and still be able to survive. Tongchang has just started planning to realize the resolution due to the requirements of the times, but the laborers have already started a strike. For a while, the public opinion is divided, with some saying that they do not care about the livelihoods of the laborers. They do not know that Mou Factory's layoffs are actually seeking its own survival, and also to give full play to the abilities of those who are not laid off, and increase their benefits. The talents bestowed by heaven are not different, only in the good use of them. If you use your talent well, the more you use it, the more obvious your ability will be. If you do not use it well, you will become lazy, and what is the use of being many? Japanese factories only need 250 laborers per 10,000 spindles, Shanghai factories need 300 laborers, and to say that the 800 laborers per 10,000 spindles in Tongchang cannot be laid off, wouldn't it be cultivating the habit of laziness, making them become useless people in the world?

Where Are the Achievements of the National Products Movement?

— Lian Ru

Although some people, driven by patriotic fervor, enthusiastically advocate for national products, there are indeed many unawakened, walking-dead compatriots, no, cold-blooded creatures; if you go to the street to take a survey, it won't take ten minutes, and I guarantee you'll get a shocking number: nine out of ten people are wearing foreign goods, especially those who consider themselves the backbone of the nation – the youth.

The passage of time cannot be stopped. More than five months of the National Products Year have already hurried by. But what are the achievements of promoting national products? How much have imports of foreign goods decreased? This is a painful matter. Please see the recent customs report:

This Year's March Excess of Imports: National Currency 101,747,420 Yuan

Last Year's January to March Excess of Imports: National Currency 185,364,862 Yuan

This Year's January to March Excess of Imports: National Currency 204,532,770 Yuan

During the National Products Year, in these days of national demise, in just three months, there has been an excess of imports of more than 204.5 million yuan. If this is extrapolated to the whole year, then this year, more than 818.18 million yuan will flow out of the country. If this money were used to buy airplanes, calculated at 150,000 yuan per plane, then 5,454 planes could be purchased.

According to investigations from various sources, the biggest reason is that people are happy to use foreign fabrics. But have the majority of people, the important figures and their concubines, capitalists and social merchants, teachers and students, truly awakened? They still need to examine themselves.

Finally, with personal enthusiasm, I implore the adults and gentlemen to use national products, to dispel my calculations, to stop just paying lip service, and to implement genuine national salvation work – promote national products. Otherwise, just wait to become slaves of a fallen nation when the Japanese soldiers arrive!

Investigation of Our Country's Calcium Carbonate Manufacturing Industry (Part 2)

— Song Lu

Investigation of Industrial Raw Materials

(2) Da Zhonghua Calcium Factory: The Da Zhonghua Calcium Factory can be considered an affiliated business of the Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory. The factory is located on Xujiahui Road, with capital increased from 100,000 to 150,000 yuan. Manager Xue Fuji has been doing business in Japan for many years and has considerable experience in the chemical industry. Manager Zhu Weichen is also very capable and decisive in his work. Xue Fuji also serves as the manager of Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory, so he often has the opportunity to inspect and experiment with the products himself. Currently, the Double Coin brand calcium carbonate produced by the factory is bright white in color and relatively pure in composition. The factory's manufacturing method was entirely imported from Japan, and now it can finally be said to have achieved "success"! The factory's output is 300 bags per day (each bag weighs 112 pounds), totaling more than 30,000 pounds. Most of it is supplied to the Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory for use, and not much is sold on the market.

(3) Xinye Chemical Factory: Xinye Chemical Factory is located at Zhaofeng Road, Rihui Port, with a separate distribution office at 692 Niuzhuang Road. Most of the factory's products are supplied to the Yisheng Rubber Factory. Chairman Feng Liansheng is a major shareholder in Yisheng Rubber Factory. Manager Chen Xiaoping worked at Mei Foo for more than ten years and is very shrewd and capable. The factory's manufacturing method is modeled after the Japanese style with some Western European elements, but it can be said that it has not yet been fully successful. The factory's output is currently 70 to 80 bags per day (each bag weighs 50 pounds), weighing approximately 4,000 pounds. In addition to being used by the Yisheng Factory to manufacture galoshes, very little is sold on the market. However, according to the factory's负责人, they plan to purchase more machinery to increase production.

In addition to the above three factories, there is also a Dali Hua Calcium Factory in Huzhou, Zhejiang, and a Bohai Chemical Factory in Tianjin, but their scale is not very large, so their output is also small. Due to space constraints, I will not describe them in detail here.

As for Japanese calcium carbonate sold in our country, because it contains one-third lime, the selling price is low. There are still many factories that do not understand chemical testing,贪图便宜, and are drinking poison to quench their thirst! According to a recent survey, the sales volume of Japanese calcium carbonate in China is still as high as 4,000 to 5,000 bags per month, accounting for about one-quarter of the total output of domestic products. On the one hand, it is hoped that our country's calcium factories will continue to work hard! On the other hand, it is especially hoped that factories purchasing enemy goods will quickly awaken themselves and switch to using domestic goods!
