Contributing Opinions

Contributions to the National Products Company

— Song Tang

Since the establishment of the China National Products Company, several months have passed in the blink of an eye, and the business is thriving, which is enough to show that the people of the country have a strong patriotic heart, which is gratifying and commendable. However, what I have heard and seen still has shortcomings, and it is like a bone stuck in my throat, eager to spit it out for relief. I humbly serve in a national products factory, and I am even more closely related, so I have to sincerely offer my advice:

(1) Pricing Issue: No matter who it is, even if they recognize and use national products, if the same type of national products have different prices, they will of course buy the cheaper one. This kind of situation is not considered strange in ordinary stores, but it is a great pity that the same product has different prices. If this happens, the customer's loss is limited, but the reputation of the National Products Company is greatly affected. Customers who come are all here for the name, and they already have a sense of trust. When they buy something and go out, they see the same type of product in the street shops selling for a lower price, wouldn't they be greatly disappointed? How can they be expected to come again? The company may not be able to carefully distinguish each item because of the many items and the busy affairs. The pricing of the National Products Company is indeed a matter of attention, and the prices of various stores on the market should be investigated and compared at any time, and then the purchase price should be calculated. If other stores can sell it, the company can do the same. It would be better if it could be lower, but at the very least, it should be based on the lowest price of each store on the market.

(2) Display of Goods: The display of goods in the National Products Company is messy and uneven. Although it is said that this is due to the busy business, it is best to browse through them at any time and fold and organize them immediately. After developing this habit, the appearance will be much better. Moreover, when customers choose goods, it is easier to deal with, and it also saves many procedures for inventory, so as to avoid wasting time.

(3) Neat Attire: As for the counter clerks and trainees who approach customers, in addition to the courtesy and attitude that should be observed, for the attire, it is not necessary to be expensive, but to be neat and clean, which should also be paid attention to by everyone.

(4) Meal Bell Reform: A friend of mine said that one day at noon, he went to the National Products Company to buy some odds and ends, and suddenly heard the bell ringing loudly. The customers didn't know why and were all panicked. When asked, it turned out to be the meal bell. If the three companies used an eight-tone steel plate, circling around once, the sound would be more elegant, and the electricity and installation costs would also be saved. The south is currently expanding. Ways should be found to change it.

(5) Discount Issue: Discount methods are the only way for stores and companies in Shanghai recently to attract customers. However, the entire great China National Products Company should have a certain period of time and should not give discounts too often. It should adhere to the principle of preferring low prices to frequent discounts, so as not to lose credibility.

Moreover, the purity and cleanliness of the quality, the agility of the packaging, and the speed and accuracy of the payment procedures are what customers hope for, and the company should pay attention to them.

National Products Introduction

Introducing the National Products Mobile Promotion Team

— Tian Ran

In this National Products Year, on the surface in Shanghai, it seems to be booming and at its peak, but everyone's goals seem to be concentrated in a few large cities, and the most numerous consumers in the villages of various places have been ignored. If you go to the countryside, you will see advertisements for enemy goods everywhere on the leaning walls and broken fences, but you can't find any propaganda for national products. Watching the import of enemy goods flowing in continuously, the cotton textiles and daily necessities used by rural farmers belong to enemy goods, accounting for more than 80%. This is such a painful thing.

Recently, several people enthusiastic about national products in Shanghai, under the guidance of the China National Products Production and Sales Cooperative Association, initiated a China National Products Mobile Promotion Team, using ships and vehicles to display samples of national products, traveling through cities, towns, and villages, so that national products can be sold well inland and penetrate into the people. Now, using two merchant ships, they are proceeding successively to the villages and towns of Jiading, Nanxiang, Taicang, Kunshan, and Changshu. The ships are equipped with the latest type of wireless radio. When traveling or arriving at a certain place, they play music at any time to attract the local people's attention. Every time the merchant ship arrives at a place, it distributes invitations, inviting people from all walks of life and business leaders to visit the ship, offering tea and snacks to induce those who love to use national products to buy. The promotion steps start with investigation. When first going to a new route for trial sales, every time it arrives at a place, the promoters go to various stores to investigate the best-selling goods and their prices and record them for reference. They also invite the people in charge of each store to visit the ship to see the samples, and offer tea and snacks to facilitate contact. At the same time, spot and order transactions are carried out. They are determined to abandon the metropolitan market and let other comrades do it, while they focus on the propaganda and promotion in the countryside, bringing national products into the people, so that they can clearly identify national products and more deeply understand the meaning of purchasing and using national products. The factories also strive to make the national products suitable for the needs of customers. The team is in the middle between the factories and the customers, so that the production and sales sides can communicate with each other. They are all very satisfied and gradually achieve the desire to eliminate all foreign goods. The team is carrying this important mission, and I am happy to introduce it.

Children's National Products Song

— Nan Gong

Good brothers, little brothers. Encourage each other, rise up together! Use national products, wear cloth clothes! Both strong and economical! Everyone must remember.

National products movement. If you want to know the details, please wait for me to use a narrative drama to illustrate!

Time: A spring dusk

Location: Puyi Society Kindergarten

Characters: Two rows of low stools are arranged in a circle, with thirty children in the front row and fifty housewives in the back row (perhaps a few ladies who are prospective housewives), Mr. Huang stands at one end of the room.

When the curtain opens, Mr. Huang has already talked about "How to Be a Parent."

Huang: I am now going to take fifteen minutes to talk to the children, okay?

Children: (Some put down their candy, some raised their tired heads, and all cheered up to listen to the development of the talk.)

Huang: What nationality are you?

Children: Chinese!

Huang: Is China strong or weak now?

A: Not very strong!

Huang: Why is China weak? I'm afraid you don't understand. Let me tell you, although there are many reasons, one of the biggest reasons is that Chinese people don't like to use Chinese goods, and the money is taken away by others.

Children: (A little silent)

Huang: Last year's battle in Zhabei, Shanghai, the rumbling cannons, have you forgotten?

Children: No!

Huang: Which country came to attack us?

Child A: The Japanese.

Huang: Why did they attack us?

Child A: Because we don't buy Japanese goods.

Huang: Why do they want us to buy Japanese goods? Let me tell you, they use Japanese goods to exchange for our money, making us poor and them rich, making us weak and them strong, and then making us perish as a poor and weak nation.

Children: (Silent for a little longer)

Huang: Which country's goods do you like?

Children: Chinese goods.

Huang: Why do you like Chinese goods?

Children: Because we are Chinese!

Huang: Good, children, Chinese people use Chinese goods! From now on, whether it's clothing, food, housing, or transportation, we will use more domestic goods, so that the country can be rich and strong, and everyone can avoid being slaves of a fallen nation!

Children: (Unanimous shout) We use Chinese goods!

Author's note: This is a fact, because it is different from general records, and there has been no opportunity to ask Mr. Huang Renzhi to revise it, so there are some imperfections in the wording, which the author is of course responsible for.

My Younger Brother's Letter

— Zhu Shanxiu

After spending my days with monotonous work, I always like to play with my little brother's photos or look at his letters; although the photos don't speak and the letters are seemingly coherent but not quite, they always eliminate my boredom invisibly. Today, as usual, I was flipping through the letter he gave me last week when my classmate Li said next to me, "Go get it, your brother has another letter. What are you doing with the old one?" I stood up to go get it, but the porter had already sent it in. Opening it up, it was written in Yan style calligraphy, with childish words, neatly written on two pages:

Brother Xiu:

Another week without greetings, I miss you very much. We have been very busy these days. Mr. Zhao, our physical education teacher, is taking us to tea shops in various villages and towns to give speeches about the harms of using foreign goods. My throat is already a little hoarse, but I don't feel any pain at all. On the contrary, I feel very happy because many people can be moved by us and nod their heads in agreement. We took this opportunity to organize a Nian Er Society, which is the name Mr. Zhao gave us. The society has established many rules: (1) Use local goods. (2) Do not smoke cigarettes. (3) Do not wear Western suits. (4) Do not apply cosmetics. Although the rules are very strict, many people have joined, and they have all sworn to practice them for life. Brother Xiu: You always dislike the ignorance of the villagers. Every time you go to the city, you must bring back some red and green foreign goods. Now that they have awakened, you can stop disliking them, right? I think they are all amiable, and they seem to be very affectionate towards me. Who says the hearts of Chinese people are dead? In addition to being role models ourselves, we continue to advise the villagers during our spare time, hoping that one day the false foreign goods will disappear. Brother Xiu: I really hope that you can also gather comrades to organize a

The propaganda team is about to set off again, goodbye.

Your beloved brother Xinnong

After reading this letter, I simply forgot the hunger pangs in my stomach. What a lovely angel he is! I still remember when he was six years old, he saw Pusheng from the neighbor's house playing with a foreign doll, and he also made a fuss about buying one. I had no choice but to buy one for him. He happily threw away his Maoshan trumpet and became friends with the foreign doll. Not long after, he accidentally fell, and his foreign doll was also crushed. He was very annoyed, and my father said, "This is a useless foreign product, do you still want it?" He quickly picked up the discarded Maoshan trumpet and turned his head without looking at the foreign doll. It has been seven years since this happened. Whenever he hears the word foreign goods, he always shows a contemptuous expression and often warns his little friends not to buy foreign goods. How could he know that we already have a Nian Er Society organization, and where did their Mr. Zhao come up with the name Nian Er Society? However, his earnest attitude is full of his words. My love for him lies in this point.

Compatriots, when you finish reading this short message that is not very smooth, you should be moved, right?

A Collection of Small Q&As

— Yi Ju

Q: Why should we use national products?

A: Because we are Chinese, so we should use national products.

Q: National products may not be as satisfactory as foreign products, right?

A: That's right, national products do have shortcomings compared to foreign products, but in terms of durability, foreign products are much inferior. Moreover, recently, national products have been gradually improving and progressing. In the future, there will always be a day when they can compete with foreign products, which is what we expect.

Q: There are some things that national products don't have, how do you explain that?

A: If there are national products, use national products. If there are no national products, use national product substitutes. Even if the price is slightly higher, you should grit your teeth and endure the pain for a while.

Q: If there really isn't any, what should we do?

A: You can not use it and try to save it. If you really can't save it, you have to buy foreign goods, but we must recognize our biggest enemy at present - Japan. No matter what, their goods must not be bought and used, and this must be remembered.

Q: If the people can all buy and use national products, will it really help the country?

A: Of course, this is absolutely unquestionable! I believe that if the people can all buy and use national products with one heart and firm will, in less than three years, they will definitely achieve great results, which depends on how hard the people work!

Q: Is it enough to just use national products? What else should we do?

A: When you are satisfied with using national products, you should widely promote their advantages among relatives and friends and persuade them to try them. The effect is ten thousand times higher than advertising. After a long time, foreign goods will inevitably be squeezed out of the market. When you are dissatisfied, you should point out the shortcomings to the producing factories and urge them to improve, so that the goods can be improved and sold without obstacles. This is the attitude that our people should have, and it also shows the degree of enthusiasm of our people in advocating national products.

Q: Where should the promotion of national products start?

A: Start with oneself, the family, and then extend to relatives and friends.

Q: Thank you, I am very grateful to you for pointing out so many good intentions.

A: It goes without saying, I am promoting national products!

A National Products Fashion in Wuxi

— Zhu Shanxiu

In Wuxi - the little Shanghai of Wuxi - your eardrums can be constantly vibrated by the majestic sound of steam whistles, most of which are emitted from yarn factories. In this way, it seems that the clothing of ordinary people in Wuxi should be devoid of imported goods. However, the reality is not what we imagine. When we walk on the street, the kind of strange clothing - especially Western suits - also constantly stabs into your eyes, making you think of the future of national products - this is really a very painful thing. Fortunately, there is now a somewhat satisfactory news, and I will introduce it to you;

Some of the Western-suited young people who still have blood in their veins have admitted their past sins. They say that they each spent at least seventy or eighty yuan of national currency a year on clothing, and they have now resolved to use national products. Therefore, recently, on the street, you can see young people wearing Shilin cloth shirts on the upper body, yellow twill Western-style trousers on the lower body - the fabrics are produced by factories such as Shenxin Qingfeng Guangqin, etc., wearing sanitary shirts from Wuhua Factory inside, and wearing basketball shoes from Brothers Company on their feet, coming and going in groups of two or three. The coolness that had already cooled down has risen again. Originally, it would be best to use national clothing styles when using national products, but please forgive them, they are already accustomed to Western clothing, and it is not an instant matter to suddenly change over. In short, this national products fashion movement may not be a ray of dawn for the future of the national products industry; to put it another way, it is better than nothing after all.

Hopes for National Products Factories

— Xu Nangong

National products have been promoted for many years, but the flood of foreign goods in the market has increased rather than decreased. The amount of excess imports in the annual customs statistics has only risen without the slightest decline. Is this because there is a lack of national product production, or because the price is high and the quality is poor? But if we go to various national product markets to observe, the various goods displayed inside, such as silk fabrics, household goods, woolen fabrics, all utensils, their superior quality and low prices, although may not be fully satisfactory, are enough to compete with imported goods. Therefore, the crux of the matter is not in production, but in the lack of widespread use. The reason for the lack of widespread use is the manufacturers' lack of effort in promotion and the lack of a spirit of unity, which is an undeniable fact.

In the past, most manufacturers were confined to one corner and did not engage in external development. Therefore, when many businesses gathered together, they caused mutual infighting due to conflicts of interest, using all their energy for overt and covert struggles among themselves, and had no time to take care of the outside world. This drawback was enough to disperse their strength. Because of the continuous internal strife, foreign goods took the opportunity to invade. Therefore, the inability of national products to be widespread, although there are various reasons for obstruction, manufacturers should bear considerable responsibility.

Therefore, we must correct the past mistakes in the future and shift the energy of fighting among businesses to external expansion, which is an urgent need for national product factories. Because of the lack of external promotion, the people have no way of knowing, and even if they want to purchase them, they do not know whether national products are produced, or even are deceived by unscrupulous merchants by changing their appearance. Therefore, the current national product factories, in addition to striving for excellence in their products, especially need to focus on publicity, such as organizing national product groups, going to various places to exhibit, so that the public can recognize them, and establishing more retail outlets to give buyers convenience, so as not to be deceived by unscrupulous merchants. They must seek to integrate production and sales to complement each other, so that national products can flow continuously and be sold throughout the country.

During this period when the call for promoting national products is permeating the country, I sincerely hope that our national product factories will change direction and take the broad road, go deep inland to promote sales, and seek our vast market. Don't just be mutually 火进 in a narrow space!

Education News

Important News

Ministry of Education Promulgates Regulations for Eligibility Verification Examinations

丨Shanghai, Beiping, Guangzhou, and Wuchang to Hold Examinations. The Ministry of Education announced on the 29th the regulations for the Eligibility Verification Examination Committee for Graduates and Undergraduates of Unregistered and Closed Private Colleges and Above, as well as the eligibility verification examination regulations, as follows:

Regulations for the Eligibility Verification Examination Committee for Graduates and Undergraduates of Unregistered and Closed Private Colleges and Above

Article 1: This committee is organized in accordance with the provisions of Article 4 of the Regulations for Eligibility Verification Examinations for Graduates and Undergraduates of Unregistered and Closed Private Colleges and Above. Article 2: This committee shall have a number of members, who shall be appointed or assigned by the Provincial and Municipal Education Bureaus from the following personnel: 1. Current presidents and teachers of public or registered private colleges and above; 2. Academic experts; 3. Current education administrative personnel. The number of committee members under item (3) shall not exceed one-fifth of the total number of committee members. Article 3: This committee shall have one chairperson, who shall preside over the affairs of the committee and shall be designated from among the committee members by the Director of the Provincial or Municipal Education Bureau. Article 4: The examination scores of candidates shall be evaluated separately by each committee member and submitted to the committee for decision. Article 5: The examination questions for each subject shall be secretly drafted by the committee members responsible for that subject and submitted to the chairperson for approval. Article 6: The evaluation of examination results shall be determined by the committee with reference to the scores of each subject and the academic qualifications of the students, and shall be submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval and publication. Article 7: This committee shall have a number of staff members for the purposes of examination supervision and numbering, who shall be assigned from among the staff of the Provincial and Municipal Education Bureaus by the Director of the Bureau. Article 8: These regulations shall be promulgated and implemented by the Ministry of Education and shall be repealed upon completion of the examination.

Regulations for Eligibility Verification Examinations for Graduates and Undergraduates of Unregistered and Closed Private Colleges and Above

Article 1: Graduates and undergraduates of unregistered and closed private colleges and above who possess one of the following qualifications at the time of admission may apply for the eligibility verification examination in accordance with these regulations: 1. Graduates of senior high schools; 2. Graduates of vocational schools equivalent to senior high school vocational courses; 3. Graduates of old-system middle schools or those who have completed one year of senior high school and two years of university preparatory courses; 4. Graduates of old-system middle schools or equivalent schools who have completed two years of service. Article 2: After registration, applicants shall undergo a qualification review. Those who do not meet the qualifications shall not be allowed to take the examination. Article 3: The qualification review shall be conducted by the qualification review committee organized by the provincial and municipal education administrative organs at the examination location. Article 4: The eligibility verification examination shall be conducted by the eligibility verification examination committee organized by the provincial and municipal education administrative organs at the examination location. The regulations for this committee shall be formulated separately. Article 5: The examination shall be divided into two categories: basic subjects and specialized subjects. The basic subjects are Party Principles, Chinese Language, Foreign Language, Social Sciences (choose one), and Natural Sciences (choose one). The specialized subjects shall be separately prescribed by the examination committee based on the level of each grade in colleges and above. Each subject shall be announced seven days before the examination period. Article 6: The evaluation of the examination results of candidates shall be based primarily on the examination and shall refer to the qualifications for assessment. If there is work experience, it may also be included for appropriate consideration. Article 7: The results of the eligibility verification examination shall be reported by the examination committee to the Ministry of Education. Graduates with superior results may be transferred to the last grade of public or registered private colleges and above when they are recruiting students (this is the result of the eligibility verification examination, and the Ministry of Education will order public and registered private colleges and above to be accommodating and not be restricted by Article 4 of the University Regulations and Article 4 of the Amended College Regulations). The remaining graduates and undergraduates shall be transferred to the corresponding grade according to their level. Article 8: Candidates whose examination results are too poor and whose academic qualifications are too shallow to be transferred to the above schools may be transferred to the corresponding grade of senior high school. Article 9: Upon completion of the examination, the Ministry of Education shall issue a transfer certificate to the candidates. Its validity is limited to the transfer and shall not be used to prove other qualifications. Article 10: When registering, applicants shall submit the following documents and handling fees: 1. Curriculum vitae, high school graduation certificate, college or university graduation certificate or certificate of completion (service certificate, if any, shall be submitted together); 2. Two recent 4-inch half-length photographs; 3. Examination handling fee of one yuan. Article 11: The registration date shall be determined by the provincial and municipal education administrative organs, but the deadline shall be June 30. Registration locations: Beiping at the Beiping Municipal Social Bureau, Shanghai at the Municipal Education Bureau, Guangzhou at the Guangdong Provincial Education Department, and Wuchang at the Hubei Provincial Education Department. Article 12: The examination locations are divided into four places: Shanghai, Beiping, Guangzhou, and Wuchang. The examination hall shall be temporarily determined by the examination committee at each location. The examination date is set to begin on July 15 simultaneously in all four places. Article 13: These regulations shall be promulgated and implemented by the Ministry of Education and shall be repealed upon completion of the examination.

Ministry of Education's Instruction

The Ministry of Education instructs the Guangdong and Hubei Education Departments and the Shanghai Education Bureau and the Beiping Social Bureau: Upon investigation, the eligibility verification examination for graduates and undergraduates of unregistered and closed private colleges and above was previously ordered by the Ministry in Instruction No. 3144 to be continued by the relevant departments (bureaus). Now, in the past year, there have been many colleges and above schools in various places that have had their registration revoked by the Ministry, or ordered to be closed in stages, or not approved for registration. The students of the above schools should be given relief. Moreover, there are not a few students in various places who, for various reasons, have been unable to participate in previous eligibility verification examinations. It is now specifically decided to hold the said examination again on July 17 of this year. In addition to separate instructions, a copy of the Regulations for Eligibility Verification Examinations for Graduates and Undergraduates of Unregistered and Closed Private Colleges and Above and the Regulations for the Eligibility Verification Examination Committee for Graduates and Undergraduates of Unregistered and Closed Private Colleges and Above are enclosed. You are instructed to prepare promptly, make a public announcement, and report the handling situation. This instruction.

General Budget for Education and Culture This Year

(Nanjing, 31st) The recurring annual expenses for education and culture this year, apart from a portion of the Boxer Indemnity funds, are the rents collected from the properties attached to the various schools, the tuition and miscellaneous fees collected by the schools, and the sales prices of publications. It is reported that the total estimated amount determined by the Ministry of Education is 2,753,587 yuan. This budget report has been sent to the Directorate General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics for inclusion in the general budget of national ordinary income for this year.

Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society to Discuss

Methods for Improving and Resolving the Chinese Economy

The 10th annual meeting of the Chinese Economic Society is scheduled to be held in Qingdao from August 21st to 28th. The board of directors has appointed Li Zhaoshi as the chairman of this year's thesis committee, with Liu Dajun and Li Shi as vice-chairmen, and Ma Yinchu, He Dekui, He Lian, Fang Ting, Shou Jingwei, Liu Binglin, Yang Duanliu, Zhu Shikang, etc. as members. The various committee members have recently agreed on a general outline for theses, which is on issues related to the improvement of the Chinese economy and their solutions. The committee's first notice has been distributed to the members, and is transcribed as follows: Since the 19th century, the European and American industrial revolutions have developed rapidly, and economic aggression has become increasingly rampant. All political and religious forces have also expanded accordingly. Our country's closed-door policy was impacted and could no longer be maintained. Seventy or eighty years ago, if the authorities had been able to clearly understand the general trend of the world, adopt new learning and advanced ideas, such as the proposals of Mr. Rong Hong, reform education, revitalize industry, seek to increase social production, and build a national economy, then our country's revitalization efforts would not have lagged behind our eastern neighbor. Moreover, if the social elites of that day had not been preoccupied with fame and wealth, but had engaged in the overall transformation of productive enterprises, and the agricultural, industrial, and commercial sectors had obtained sufficient talent to actively promote development, then in the world's economic evolution, our Chinese nation would not have fallen behind to this extreme. Only Korea, which had regarded the national economy and people's livelihood at that time, eventually suffered from the oppression and aggression of imperialists and could do nothing about it. This is something we cannot help but feel deeply saddened about. In the past, Mr. Sun Yat-sen, recognizing this, advocated the Principle of People's Livelihood and promoted the Industrial Plan, deeply desiring to fundamentally remedy this collapsing national economy, but he passed away before seeing its implementation. Those in the know say that his plan has recently been tested in Soviet Russia and has achieved obvious results. In our country, it is even more urgent to seek its realization. Economy is the driving force behind all undertakings. All aspects of livelihood, politics, education, construction, and national defense rely on the economy for advancement. Therefore, in modern times, countries often use economic aggression to develop their national power. The importance of the economy has surpassed that of politics. Now, within our country, the people's livelihood is in decline, and externally, we are surrounded by strong enemies, and the economic decline is indescribable. We do not need to talk about international development, but to seek appropriate survival and establish ourselves in the world's progress, the transformation of the economy cannot be delayed. These are all the responsibilities of us economists. Therefore, we propose that the general outline of the annual meeting's theses be "Issues and Solutions for the Current Economic Transformation of China." We hope that the members of the society will express their great opinions on this issue for discussion, so that we can use it to establish a great cause of economic revolution and lay the foundation for a strong and prosperous nation. We earnestly urge you to do so. This announcement.

It is reported that all correspondence from the society's thesis committee is received and forwarded by the National Jiaotong University on Haige Road in Shanghai. As of today, more than ninety members of the society have registered with the headquarters to attend the meeting. At that time, the members from the South will gather in Nanjing to travel north together, and the members from the North will gather in Jinan to travel east on the Jiaoji Railway with the members from the South. It is also reported that the society will take the opportunity to inspect the rural construction in Shandong, which has achieved remarkable results, and will invite Qingdao Mayor Shen, Liang Shuming, Wu Dingchang, and Chen Guangfu, the organizers of rural construction in Shandong, to give speeches. The society's headquarters will also present a thesis entitled "Utilization of Foreign Capital and Technology," which will be read by the president's representative. The Hangzhou branch will present a thesis entitled "The Pathological Conditions of Zhejiang's Rural Economy and Their Remedies," which will be read by the branch's directors. However, the topic proposed by the Shanghai branch is still unknown. The majority of the society's members are in Shanghai, and it is expected that they will also present a similar thesis.

Local News

Health Education Exhibition Opens Today

Opening Ceremony at Puyi Society at 10:00 AM

Second Venue Set Up at Cangji Primary School on Zhonghua Road

Free Dental Checkups for Children During the Exhibition

The citywide first health education exhibition, jointly organized by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau and the Health Bureau, is now fully prepared and will begin today for a period of three days. The first venue is located at Puyi Society on Zixia Road, Dadongmen, Nanshi, and the second venue is located at Cangji Primary School on Zhonghua Road. The opening ceremony will be held at Puyi Society at 10:00 AM today, presided over by Mayor Wu, the president of the association, and Directors Pan and Li, the vice presidents. The details are recorded as follows:

A Glimpse of the Exhibits: 190 schools participated in this exhibition on a voluntary basis, with 24 experimental schools. More than 20 social groups and reference groups participated, with a total of more than 12,000 exhibits. The Ministry of Health transported a large number of valuable items to Shanghai for display. Other organizations, such as the China Leprosy Relief Association, the National Anti-Drug Association, the China Health Education Association, and the Commercial Press, also displayed valuable items. The life photos of Songxue Primary School and the fetal development specimens of Renhe Obstetrics and Gynecology Hospital are rare exhibits.

Exhibition Arrangements: Due to the large number of exhibits, Puyi Society was insufficient for display, so a second venue was added at Cangji Primary School. The staff of the planning department, Shao Rugan, Ding Shoutang, Zhang Meisun, Cheng Fengxiang, Chen Hanming, etc., worked all night for days and nights and completed the arrangement last night. The first venue displays exhibits from elementary schools and kindergartens and exhibits from social groups in homes on the three floors with a total of eleven classrooms and two corridors. The bottom floor displays exhibits from the experimental group of elementary schools. The second floor displays exhibits from the voluntary participation group. The disorderly exhibits from families are displayed on the third floor. The second venue displays exhibits from the middle school group of schools, exhibits from the social group's infectious disease group and anti-drug group, and exhibits from the reference group, with a total of ten classrooms.

Conference Program: The program is as follows: (1) Free bathing for infants (one to three years old) from 1:00 PM to 5:00 PM every day; (2) Free cholera vaccination and smallpox vaccination every day in the morning and afternoon; (3) Health lectures every afternoon; (4) Children's health activities and health movies every morning and afternoon; (5) Public health knowledge lectures on the afternoon of June 1st, health education lectures for teachers and staff on the afternoon of the 2nd, and children's healthy habits lectures on the afternoon of the 3rd.

Today's Performances: 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM: Hell and Heaven (Jingye Elementary School), Health Dance (Shangwen); 11:00 AM to 12:00 PM: Two Nurses on the Battlefield, Doing This Every Day (Bide); 1:00 PM to 2:00 PM: The Road to Health, Finding Friends (Xunxing); 2:00 PM to 3:00 PM: Group Rope Meeting (Shihua), Toothbrush Exercises (First Experimental Elementary School); 3:00 PM to 4:00 PM: Health Lecture; 4:00 PM to 5:00 PM: Fitness Dance, The Doll is Sick Skit (Wuben Elementary School).

Visitor Information: (1) Proceed in order, do not retreat; (2) Do not bring items into the venue; (3) Do not touch; (4) Do not make noise; (5) Do not smoke; (6) Spit into the basin; (7) Walk in order; (8) Please leave the venue immediately when the bell rings for closing.

Venue Guide: (1) First venue of the exhibition: Puyi Society, second venue: Cangji Elementary School; (2) Performance venue: outdoor reed shed in Puyi Society; (3) Lecture hall: same as above; (4) Movie theater: No. 9 on the bottom floor of Puyi Society; (5) Rest and reception room: No. 102 on the bottom floor of Puyi Society; (6) Exhibition office: Information desk downstairs in Puyi Society; (7) Vaccination, dental checkups, and injections: injection station at the entrance of Puyi Society; (8) Bathing: No. 30 on the third floor of Puyi Society.

Dental Checkups: Children who visit the exhibition can voluntarily request a dental checkup. If any defects are found, they can go to the Shanghai Nanshi Education Bureau, Zhabei Feihong Elementary School, Gaoqiao Health Experimental Institute and other children's dental clinics for free treatment. The association has contacted the Family Industry Society to provide appropriate prizes for children with excellent teeth. The checkup matters will be handled by dental officer Su Jielang of the Health Bureau.

Philippine Scout Group Requests Speech from Mayor Wu

The Group Will Visit the Zhabei War Zone Today

Participate in Aircraft Naming Ceremony This Afternoon

A delegation of the Philippine Chinese Boy Scouts, consisting of 54 people, led by group leader Wu Zongmu, departed from the Philippines on the 9th of this month to return to China to investigate the customs and human relations of the motherland. They passed through Shanghai and went to Beijing, where they stayed for two weeks. They then went to Hangzhou to participate in the Boy Scout Review Conference, and arrived in Shanghai from Hangzhou on the 29th. Yesterday morning at 10:30 AM, accompanied by members of the Municipal Scout Council, the entire delegation went to the Municipal Government to request a speech from Mayor Wu. Mayor Wu gave a speech in the conference hall of the Municipal Government for about twenty minutes, mainly encouraging the delegation with cautionary words. It is learned that the delegation is scheduled to visit the war zones of January 28th, Wusong, Jiangwan, and Zhabei today, and will participate in the naming ceremony of the first aircraft of Shanghai Municipality this afternoon. It is reported that the delegation will stay in Shanghai for three to five days before returning to the Philippines.

Municipal Education Bureau Bans Huxi Elementary School in Shanghai

Huxi Elementary School, located at the intersection of Tangjiawan and Xilin Road, Huxi, was previously ordered by the Education Bureau to improve, but it has not complied at all. Recently, after the Education Bureau received complaints and sent personnel to investigate, it found that the school's management was corrupt and its facilities were simple, making it difficult to improve. It has sent a letter to the French Concession Public Bureau and the Second Special District Local Court to send police to order its closure to avoid misleading children.

丨Men's Basketball: District One Wins Over District Two

At 4:00 PM on the 31st, the men's basketball final between District One and District Two took place. District One's team was primarily composed of players from the National West Lake Art Academy, while District Two centered around Chunhui Middle School. District One displayed refined technique and excellent passing. At 4:00 PM sharp, District One led with a score of 20 to 9 in the first half. After fierce competition in the second half, the final score was 49 to 21, with District One winning and securing the basketball championship.

Preliminary Round: District Two Wins Over District Three On the afternoon of the 30th, at 3:00 PM, District Two and District Three competed at the provincial sports field. District Two was a combined team of Ning County residents and Chunhui Middle School, boasting rich experience. District Three mainly consisted of high school students from Jinhua Provincial Seventh Middle School, who had fewer opportunities for practice and observation, resulting in weaker overall strength. The competition turned out to be one-sided, with a score of 47 to 14, District Two won decisively. The referee was Hu Weiyue.

District Two's team was entirely composed of players from Shangyu's Chunhui Middle School. 丨Football: District One Wins Big Over District Two

Only District One and District Two participated in the football competition, and the outcome would determine who won the championship. The match started at 3:00 PM sharp on the afternoon of the 30th. District One's team was a selection of elite players from the Aviation and Zhejiang University, full of talent, all of whom were college students, making their strength formidable. District Two centered around the Linhai Public Team, supported by strong players from Baima Lake Chunhui Middle School on either side, making their strength also quite considerable.

First Half: 4 to 0　About ten minutes into the game, Liu Shizan, a short and stout general from District One, received a pass from the rear and scored the first goal with one kick, greatly boosting morale. Facing this dangerous situation, District Two still worked hard to hold on. After about twenty minutes, the stout Liu, again aided by Xue Yongyuan's pass, scored the second goal. Xue Yongyuan then scored a third goal, but it was disallowed due to offside. District Two's goal was fraught with danger, and Xue Yongyuan took advantage again, continuing to hit the target twice. At halftime, District One led 4 to 0.

Second Half: 3 to 3　After the break, District Two regrouped and returned to the field with renewed spirit. After ten minutes of intense play, Jin Huaizhi of District One dribbled deep into the field and scored another goal with a powerful kick. District Two, having traveled from afar, feared being shut out and losing face, so they tried to counterattack. Jian Jiang Qiu Fei of District Two, with the support of Wang Xinxing, shot directly into the net. District Two's team felt like they had taken a dose of stimulant, and their voices shook with vigor, scoring another goal. Jin Huaizhi, District One's speedy forward, was furious and charged forward, successfully scoring a goal. District Two, not wanting to be outdone, launched another attack, shooting fiercely from the corner. Wang Shiduo, District One's goalkeeper, saved five or six dangerous shots, making invaluable contributions. Finally, Wang Xinxing of District Two scored with a long-range shot that the goalkeeper couldn't save. In the second half, District Two had the upper hand with a score of 3 to 2. Overall, District Two maintained a consistent spirit and deserved praise even in defeat. The final score was 6 to 3, with District One winning the championship. The referee was Gao Shangzhi.

American Invents Unbreakable Javelin

(Washington Electric News) The wood used to make javelins for track and field competitions in various countries around the world is not uniform and is not strong, so it is easy to break in the middle of the competition, which is very uneconomical. Now, an employee of the University of Washington in the United States has invented an unbreakable javelin made of fir wood. It has been used several times by the school's track and field coach, Mr. Yan Mengte Sun, who threw it on cement and brick ground for testing, and it was not damaged at all. Now the school plans to request the World Athletics Federation to recognize this javelin and order countries around the world to imitate and use it.

Shanghai Sports Field Amateur Basketball Team Wins乙Group Championship

The Shanghai Sports Field Amateur Basketball Tournament held its final match yesterday, with the best team in乙Group One, Kang Yuan, and the best team in乙Group Two, Jianmei, competing for the championship and runner-up of the乙Group. Ten to Five

Preparation of the Shanghai Cycling Association

Recently, Henry A. G. Keates, Parcy J. G. Bew, and William A. G. Waters, considering that cycling is used for exercise in Western countries and is a very popular sport, but it is rarely promoted in China, in order to encourage people from all walks of life to develop an interest in cycling, they initiated the Shanghai Cycling Association. The preparatory meeting was held at the Ann Lun Company at No. 39 Tongfu Road at 6:00 PM the other day. Tang Yijun was elected as president, Mr. Kcates as honorary secretary and treasurer, and it was decided that the association's office would be temporarily located in the Ann Lun Company. The membership fee is provisionally set at 3 yuan for this year until the end of the year, and 5 yuan per year from next year. All members will be able to enjoy free participation in the association's social events or competitions in the future. On that day, new members joined one after another, totaling more than 20 people, including two female members from the West. It is said that a formal inaugural meeting will be held soon, to be held in a public place. People from all walks of life who are interested in cycling, regardless of gender, age, or occupation, are welcome to join the association. Please contact Mr. Tang Guanyi at Ann Lun Company, No. 39 Tongfu Road.

Free Talk

Wind

— Cao Juren

I have heard that complaints are close to being reactionary, and it is not appropriate to express them too much; wind and moon are a bit corrupt, and this matter must also be taken seriously. In the early years of the Western Jin Dynasty, the Eight Princes fought fiercely, causing turmoil in the world; Liu Yao and Shi Le shouted, and they entered Luoyang ten times. If you flip through the Book of Jin Dynasty, what kind of praise or criticism do you see from the historians? Alas! The imperial court was originally free from mistakes, and the troublemakers were Wang (Bi) and He (Yan). Wang and He advocated pure talk and liked to talk about wind and moon, so they were accused of "causing benevolence and righteousness to decline, scholars to be disgraced, rituals to collapse, and the Central Plains to fall apart." In the future, if the historians accuse the loss of Rehe and the crisis in Tianjin and Beijing, it is because the editors of Free Talk talk too much about wind and moon. To correct the law and extend the national law, what will you do? There is also a master of talking about wind and moon, Wang Yifu, everyone accuses the demise of the Western Jin Dynasty as his "verbal fault"; Shi Le caught him and stated his crimes; "This person is the one who disturbs the world!" In the future, if the king's army goes south and all people submit, the holy king will punish the two opinions, and the Free Talk reporters will have nowhere to escape their guilt to the world, so talking more about wind and moon, I am quite skeptical!

So, is it okay not to talk about "wind and moon" and only talk about "wind"? When I open the Book of Songs, oh my god, it's even worse! The Great Preface to the Book of Songs says; "Wind is wind... The superiors use wind to transform the inferiors, and the inferiors use wind to satirize the superiors, focusing on the text while indirectly admonishing, those who speak are not guilty, and those who hear are enough to be cautious, so it is called wind." We lowly people can only satirize the superiors with wind; I'm afraid that the superiors will be unhappy, and the words in my heart are spoken in a roundabout way, desperately working on focusing on the text and indirectly admonishing; as a result, those who speak are still guilty, and those who hear are not cautious. It also makes the orthodox thinkers greatly unhappy, saying that "satirizing the superiors with wind" and "focusing on the text and indirectly admonishing" are not open and aboveboard, and are so unacceptable that they itch to take a bite. So, I am cautious about talking about "wind" alone.

Moreover, the word "wind" has another meaning. The Oath of Fei; "Horses and cattle in the wind", Zuo Zhuan: "Horses and cattle do not meet in the wind", Fu Qian noted; "Females and males attract each other is called wind." Guangya and Shiming explain "wind, release." Han Shu Yiwen Zhi notes; "Release, dissolute." Saying "females and males attract each other", saying "release", saying "dissolute", all have the meaning of licentiousness and recklessness; When moral education is written in the orders, customs are cultivated, it will never tolerate excessive and unrestrained behavior; the reasons why "wind" cannot be discussed are like this.

Some say: "The southern wind is warm", "benevolent wind is widely spread", "good weather and good harvest", there are many auspicious words, why not praise the holiness of Yao and Shun, and praise the benevolence of Wen and Wu? Why satirize with wind? Cao Zi said: "Yes, yes, I will praise it:" The poem says:

"The north wind is roaring, the rain and snow are falling: Show kindness and love to me, hold hands and go home, how empty and evil, how urgent and just!

Nothing red is not a fox, nothing black is not a crow, show kindness and love to me, hold hands and go by car, how empty and evil, how urgent and just!"

(Poem: Northern Wind)

Dismissal

— Peng Xuezhen

This morning, Rongzi went out and returned with a sad face not long after.

Mother was mending clothes on the threshold, watching Rongzi enter the house, her heart skipped a beat, and she almost pricked her finger with the needle.

"What's wrong, can't you really weave anymore?"

"I told you long ago, the silkworm leaves that cost more than a dollar a load last year, the cocoons sold for thirty dollars a load, the sellers are heartbroken, and after deducting the cost of seeds and labor, there's not much left; but the silk factory is weaving silk and can't sell it, everyone loves to wear foreign goods."

"Did Uncle San's workshop close down?"

"Haven't quite a few closed down in recent years? It's all the mess caused by rayon."

Rongzi remembered Uncle San's bitter face:

"There's no more silk today, my workshop will stop working from now on."

"You're having an old episode again, I've heard you say it ten times?"

"This time it's true, I heard that some have lost all their money, the woven silk can't be sold, and Hongsheng Silk Factory won't take it. They say the Japanese are fighting us somewhere, it can't be transported out, and the people are poor."

"But wearing foreign goods doesn't make them poor! What, what are we going to eat? Yirongzi was really anxious, staring straight ahead.

"Ask you, I want to go back to my hometown, but the fields, even paying the rent isn't enough, how many people in our village had enough to eat last year?" The old man's voice was also low.

Rongzi also remembered the scene of five or six companions coming out of the workshop with their heads downcast: there was no longer the rattling noise, that dark little room, that low-lying mud and dilapidated large wooden machines, everything was as nostalgic as the winter sun, and even that musty smell was strangely endearing today.

But everyone left silently, leaving behind the wooden machines that Uncle San would probably chop up for firewood when it rained heavily. Second Auntie vaguely stroked her chest, looking at the door.

It seems that one day won't let us live, Xiuma, what will we eat tomorrow?

The woman opened the quilt and dug under the bed a little. A handful of copper coins, 490 of them, scattered on top, and big tears fell on them.

Early Summer in Shanghai

— Perhaps

The spring breeze seems to have mischievously slipped away like a naughty child.

Light, joyful smiles fall from the lips of passersby, silently, imperceptibly, into the dust of the road. Sunlight shines on the backs of young men in flannel suits, tickling them as if women's fingernails were lightly scratching them.

At noon, the sidewalks seem a little deserted. The shop assistants, leaning against the glass counters, rub their sleepy eyes, glaring disapprovingly at the oblivious trams. The usually silent coffee shops, like widows preparing to remarry, are adorned with unusual beauty, and the signs outside the doors for soda, ice cream... are even more eye-catching than the red characters in a certain newspaper during the January 28th Incident. Behind the window curtains, in the clean seating area, pairs of young lovers sit, sucking shaved ice with straws, smiling. The boy hides in the corner, secretly laughing.

The passengers on the bus route have been particularly crowded recently, and the number of visitors to Zhaofeng Park has broken all previous records.

The poor ghosts living in the slums seem to have been saved, smiling as they take their winter clothes to the pawnshop.

The pot-bellied capitalists are beginning to worry, even furrowing their brows in their dreams.

The young mistresses, confined in their Western-style houses, idly tease their Pekingese dogs, wasting their endless days. Their souls fly out of their bodies, searching for their…… beneath the white clouds.

The weather changes day by day, and everyone's mood changes day by day.

After eight o'clock, black-plated cars rush madly into the French Concession. Dignified English gentlemen, in the darkness of the carriages, steal kisses on the bare breasts of young girls. The drivers mutter and curse the drunken sailors who are embracing saltwater sisters and singing in the middle of the road.

On Avenue Joffre, young men and women are immersed in dreams of love and poetry. The white…, leaning against the lamppost, silently recalls the Gao… of his homeland before 1917.

Mount Lu? Mount Mogan? … The quarreling of the compradore and his concubine drifts down from the terrace.

"Am I like a bird in a cage?" The weary sigh of a traveler asking at the western pavilion.

The tram speeds past, the platform crowded with people, taking an economic joyride.

"Peace talks in Peiping and Tientsin have been concluded!" The newspaper boy at the tram stop cries out in a shrill voice.

However, like a stone thrown into surging waves, no one pays attention. The trembling breasts of women in thin gauze, bare feet, and lotus-like pink arms captivate the hearts of passersby.

The entire early summer Shanghai is intoxicated with a carnal atmosphere.

Random Jottings from Qu Lu

— Zi Zhan

(Thirty-Seven) I Can't Help But Write a Poem

When Cangjie created writing, the ghosts were said to have wept,

Is it not without reason that writing invites jealousy?

Scholars do not fear the crime of wild words,

Poets would rather not cease their feelings of anger and indignation.

Willing to talk about strange water creatures with a single spine,

Still willing to be imprisoned in the mountains for ten years.

Pitying the masses who go alone to the southern wilderness,

The sea of clouds is vast, and the path of the world is long.

Zhigang came from Peiping and is about to travel to western Guangdong. He passed through Shanghai and we were able to meet again for a few days. He showed me his recent book, "An Exploration of the Myths of Chinese Water Gods," and I read it to the end. Such an obscure subject, with such tedious research, can make the reader feel like they are reading a fluent essay or a vivid novel. It is truly an unprecedented work in the study of Chinese folklore, which will be validated by peers, and is not just my personal opinion. Zhigang is about to leave. Li Wu Juren said that I should write a poem, so I can't help but recite one first, to await the sounds of others. Moreover, with mutual understanding between China and Japan, the world will be at peace from now on, and it is also indispensable for we muddle-headed and senile poets to embellish such a prosperous age.

Carrot Top Whiskers

— Written by Jules Kenaro, Translated by Lin Qu

Selected Correspondence Between Carrot Top Whiskers and His Father

Carrot Top Whiskers' Letter to Di Bick (Sent from Saint Mark's Academy):

Dear Dad,

My fishing game during the holidays has made me sick. I feel like some big nails have grown out of my sides. I'm now sick in bed. I'm lying on my back, and the nurse is putting plasters on me. When the nails haven't broken through yet, I feel pain. After they break through, I don't feel it anymore. But these nails are breeding like chickens. After healing one, three new ones grow out. But I hope this problem will be gone soon.

Lei Xu Ke's Reply:

Dear Carrot Top Whiskers,

Since you are now preparing to celebrate your first Catholic initiation and studying mathematical catechism, you should know that humanity does not want you to bring nails to them. Jesus Christ had nails on his hands and feet. His nails were real, but he didn't complain.

Be brave! Your Father

Carrot Top Whiskers' Letter to Dian Bick:

Dear Dad, I have good news for you: I grew a tooth. Although it's not the age yet, I think it's a precocious tooth. I believe a second one will grow next. I will continue to work hard and abide by the rules to comfort you.

Lei Bick's Reply:

Dear Carrot Top Whiskers, Just as your tooth was growing, one of my teeth began to shake. It didn't fall out resolutely until yesterday. Therefore, although you have one more tooth, your father has one less. So the total number of teeth in our family remains the same, without any increase or decrease.

Carrot Top Whiskers' Letter to Lei Bick:

Dear Dad, I'll tell you something, see if you can imagine it: Yesterday was the birthday of our Latin teacher, Mr. Zhe Ke, and the whole class had already unanimously elected me to deliver a congratulatory speech. I was flattered and spent a lot of effort preparing the speech, and I appropriately quoted a few Latin sentences in it. To be immodest, I was very satisfied with this speech myself. I copied it clearly on a piece of parchment. Yesterday, encouraged by my classmates whispering, "Go, go quickly!" I ran in front of his podium while Mr. Zhe Ke wasn't paying attention. But as soon as I unfolded the congratulatory speech and read aloud:

Respected Mr.,

Zhe Ke stood up angrily and shouted:

"Get back to your seat!"

You can imagine how I ran back to my seat with a broken heart. While my classmates were hiding their faces behind their books, Mr. Zhe Ke angrily ordered me:

"Translate this passage of Latin for me."

Dear Dad, what are your thoughts on this matter?

Lei Bick's Reply to Carrot Top Whiskers:

Dear Carrot Top Whiskers, when you become a member of parliament, you will see many of the same things. Everyone has their own duties. Since people have placed your teacher on the podium, it is obvious that he is there to speak, not to listen to you speak. (To be continued)

Spring and Autumn

Qian Li and Li Wa

— Zhan Lu

Heavily made up with a lot of powder, dressed娇娇滴滴娇娇滴滴, giving speeches to the public to resist Japan and save the country. The two words "Leng Qianli" are derived from Wu Gan, meaning to dress up and beautify. Women in Wu

The school said a few cold words, calling out: "Resisting Japan does not forget emotions, Qianli can also resist Japan."

Therefore, the ancient name of Suzhou was "Liwa Township." In this year of severe national crisis, the Liwa transformation of Suzhou women is "greater than, and not less than" in the past. The Liwa transformation of the red and plain daughters, the Liwa transformation of the red and plain daughters of the wealthy families, the Liwa transformation of the young women of the rich families, that's all; there are also the Liwa transformation of the Xiaojia Biyu, and the Liwa transformation of the small vendors. Even, relying on the omnipotence of Qianli, it seems that it can move the retrograde of the era; there are Liwa-style middle-aged women who forget that they are 20 years old, and Liwa-style white-bearded grandmothers who forget that they are 30 years old. Whether Liwa is beautiful or not, let's deal with it later; but, Liwa's only mission is nothing more than being a salesman for enemy goods. On the bodies of various Liwa who love Qianli, they must always sell some "Nine People" brand products.

Female Bodhisattvas, female Bodhisattvas, I put my hands together and offer a word: You love Qianli, then Qianli; you love to be Liwa, then be Liwa; this is your freedom, which is useless. But, you must know that studying your Qianli method from domestic products is true Qianli; creating your Liwa on domestic products is true Liwa. Female Bodhisattvas, female Bodhisattvas, believe in this statement, immeasurable merit.

Random Notes on Reading History

— Long Sao

The collapse of the Ming Dynasty was purely due to the court being filled with mediocre and corrupt officials. Ma Shiying and Ruan Dacheng, taking advantage of the situation of partial peace, used the name of Prince Fu to act against the famous scholars of Fushe, such as Gu Gao, and finally monopolized power and became昏憒昏憒. Once the Qing army reached Nanjing, Ma was killed, and Ruan Dacheng sued for peace and attacked Xianxia Ridge and died. Ni Ruixuan, a woman from Suqian, scolded: "Selling the country still sells oneself, it's a pity to call a traitor a gentleman!" Extremely painful. Compared with Cao Cao's cunning and smoothness, and his broad spirit, he is really not on the same level. But in the world, there are still traitors like Ma and Ruan!

At that time, Grand Sima Yao Xuesen, seeing that the Ming Dynasty was about to end, wrote on a friend's "Monkey Holding Vine Sleeping on a Dead Tree Picture", there is a sentence: The monkey should wake up now, don't wait until the vine is dry and the tree falls 丨丨丨But the monkey didn't wake up after all, and after the tree fell, Ma and Ruan, who ruined the country, finally died. The mirror of selling the country is like this.

Historian Hendrik Vanloon, in The Story of Mankind, most succinctly describes the fall of Rome: Most of the people were gluttonous, lazy, and indulgent, and they didn't know at all about the country's impending destruction; the young people in the country, because they couldn't afford the heavy taxes, all joined the army to seek the interests of ambitious emperors, they lived in war from birth to death, the emperors of the second and third centuries all came from the army, relying on the strength of the brothers in the barracks, they drove out the previous emperor and replaced him; soon, they were also ousted from the palace by another warrior; thus the city became ruins, the people starved and plundered, and commerce also stopped, … the country was divided up by the nearby small nations! After reading this passage, we turned to examine our own country, the people not only don't know about politics, but also can't know, and are not allowed to know; young people drift around in the city with nothing to do, so they drop their pens, take up guns, and fill the tools of civil war; just looking at the situation in all aspects is no different from Rome in the twilight of 476!

Remembering the Martyrs Cemetery of the May Thirtieth Movement

— Rong Yu

Because the May Thirtieth period is approaching, and this May Thirtieth Cemetery is opposite my humble abode, so on a certain evening, I strolled over to pay my respects. Seeing the old wounds in the yellow earth; remembering the new scars on the edge of the Great Wall, it really makes people feel indescribable叹无方叹无方, and they don't know whether to laugh or cry.

Speaking of the May Thirtieth Cemetery, it is less than half a mile north of the Eight Character Bridge. During the January 28th Incident two years ago, the area around this tomb was the site of fierce battles between the two armies. Even today, there are still grass-covered trenches left; like honeycomb-like bullet marks. The cemetery covers an area of more than ten acres and is surrounded by low walls. At the entrance is a high altar where inscriptions are placed. In the center are four large characters "Those who come, do not forget," written by the late President of the Executive Yuan Tan Yankai. There is also an inscription next to it, written by Mr. Cai Yuanpei and written by Mr. Yan Shenyu. The article is nothing more than mourning the dead and encouraging them to come, so I will not repeat it!

After taking a few dozen steps further, there is the martyrs' tomb. That tomb is built very delicately. A flat platform more than ten feet high is built of cement, with stone steps in the middle for climbing. The platform is five or six feet long and six or seven feet wide, with stone benches on both sides for resting. In the center is the raised tomb. At the top of the tomb stands a…, crowing towards the east. Is it calling out to awaken the dreams of military force in the eastern neighborhood? Or is it calling us to wake up from our drunken lives? But I dare to say: Rooster! It's a waste of your good intentions!

Behind the stone steps, there is a hidden cave that leads directly to the place where the coffin is placed. However, it is dark and light inside, and you must hold an electric torch and candlelight to enter. Moreover, it is not very ventilated, and the moldy and humid air makes people want to vomit. Twelve coffins are arranged horizontally in the middle, which are the martyrs who sacrificed themselves on Nanjing Road!

Next to the tomb is a row of three-room bungalows, which are used for sacrifices. An old woman who guards the tomb is sitting at the door, and she is very happy to talk. She said to me: "During the January 28th Incident two years ago, because I didn't have the capital to escape, I hid in the tomb day and night. The tomb is surrounded by thick cement, as strong as a fortress, and bullets and small shells cannot move it in the slightest. As long as there is food and fuel inside, there is really nothing to worry about. Later, a team of soldiers used it as a temporary headquarters, eating, drinking, singing, and talking were very lively, so I cooked for them, and I really forgot that bullets were flying outside the tomb. Later, when our army retreated and the Japanese army came, they didn't make things difficult for me because I was old and alone; and they paid deep respect to the heroic souls in the tomb.

Heroic souls in the tomb! Are you sleeping soundly underground, with your eyes closed and your hearts dead? The ravages of Zhabei two years ago have already made you uneasy. Now looking back north, it makes you even more resentful! Cry! Cry! Green grass and white poplars are also weeping sadly; crows and frogs are also呜呜地哀呜呜呜呜呜呜呜地哀鸣!

Preface to the Catalogue of Mr. Liu Haisu's European Tour Works Exhibition

— Sun Ke

Chinese and Western painters both value transmission, and because they value transmission, there is a patriarchal system. Disciples do not necessarily fall behind their teachers. Understanding it is up to the individual. Therefore, one sect can be derived into several schools, and one school can be derived into several branches. There are sects in schools and branches in branches, almost like the Buddhist inheritance. If you want to stand out in the art world, but there is nothing to inherit from above, you must rely on which branch or school your work is close to. If you are not like this, you will not be able to convince people, and people will also criticize you as water without a source or a tree without roots. Mr. Liu Haisu is a genius, but he believes that this is living under someone else's roof. Even if you become famous, the name is not my name, even if you become a family, the family is not my family. Therefore, he cultivates his energy, concentrates his spirit, and silently operates it. He gathers his nature and restrains his emotions, and thinks deeply about it. He goes far to the East and West Oceans to watch it wantonly. Everything that the beasts walk, the birds fly, the fish swim, the grass and trees are beautiful, the clouds and clouds are steaming, the high cliffs and deep valleys, the ancient garrisons and cold cities, everything in the universe that is playable, entertaining, surprising, appalling, singable, and weeping, is stored in the chest. After storing it for a long time, there is a sudden understanding in the heart, and then it is generously released from the hand. With or without measure, it merges with things, without knowing there is a sect, let alone a branch. Therefore, he called himself an art rebel. Those who hear the name may doubt that he is not ancient, not modern, not Chinese, not Western, and that he cannot achieve anything. They don't know that you want to be neither ancient nor modern, neither Chinese nor Western, but to become yourself. Western poet saint Byron said, man is great, but nature is greater. Your becoming yourself is to make yourself one with nature. Its greatness is beyond humanity. Mencius said: Those who wait for King Wen to rise up are ordinary people. Those who are limited by patriarchal branches, how can they talk about this? I heard that there is also a sudden enlightenment method in Buddhism. Are you an enlightened person? I would like to tell this to those who read your paintings.

Novel

The Northeastern Fourth Company Commander

— Zhang Henshui

Episode 8: Angry words inspire the youth to resign from office and escape.

Enthusiastically pitying the girl, he comes to hug her.

Gui Zhi shook her head, shaking the two long earrings on her ears, and hit her face a few times, pouting and smiling: I don't know! After saying these four words, he walked into the inner room. Mr. Jiang and Company Commander Guan sat across a table, pushing the teacup again and smiling: It's really slow to come to our house. There's nothing to eat or drink. Guan Yaowu said: I ate and drank in the backyard, and I don't need it now. I came here specifically to pay a New Year's visit. Mr. Jiang was tapping copper coins from his clothes while saying: If you don't eat or drink, you should smoke two cigarettes. Guan Yaowu shook his hand repeatedly and said: I don't want to smoke cigarettes either. I'll wait for the day when our cousin gets married, and I'll come back to drink a glass of happy wine with you. Mr. Jiang smiled and said: You always mention this sentence. Do you really want to be a matchmaker for your cousin? Or are you just joking? Guan Yaowu said: Really! How could it be just a joke? Gui Zhi was sitting alone on the pit in the room, peeling his fingers with both hands, listening to what was being said outside. Now that he heard Guan Yaowu say that he was really acting as a matchmaker, he couldn't help but feel his heart jump twice. So he sat a little closer to the wall, tilted his ears, and listened to the next door. At this time, Guan Yaowu's voice suddenly became quieter, whispering, and he didn't know what he was talking about. Because his voice was low, his own mother's voice was also low. It seemed that Mr. Jiang said something like, what else are we unwilling to do? When Gui Zhi heard these words, his heart was beating even more. However, he didn't figure out what he was saying, and he didn't know if he was talking about himself. In this ambiguous situation, he couldn't object even if he wanted to. If his mother didn't admit it, he would be said to be thinking too much. As a girl, thinking too much about marriage is indecent. Therefore, when he wanted to listen but couldn't openly listen, he lay horizontally on the pit, turned his face, and fell asleep quietly. In fact, he was also listening to the people outside the house. (86)

Small Recipe

Early Summer Fish

— Zhu Qingyi

"Fish is what I want." Mr. Feng, who was a boarder under Lord Mengchang's door, couldn't help complaining because he watched the whole fresh fish being sent to other people's tables, and he couldn't even taste a drop of fish soup. Leaning on the pillar, he flicked his sword and shouted: "Should I return with my long sword? I have no fish to eat!" Yes, fish is indeed delicious; the perch of Songjiang and the carp of the Yellow River are really famous fish known throughout the country, and the vinegar fish of Hangzhou is an even more famous delicacy on the shore of West Lake. In this early summer season, it is the time when brocade scales are on the market. What is recorded below are all seasonal fish in the Jiangnan cookbook.

Soft-shelled turtle Soft-shelled turtle is the common name for 鳖. When peonies are blooming, it is the most popular time for soft-shelled turtles. Its taste is fresh, rich, and delicious, just right, and is called "Peony Soft-Shelled Turtle." After this time, it will be too old to eat and become "Old and yellowed pearls are worthless." Although soft-shelled turtles are called fish, they are reptiles with shells and feet. Its skirt is not only rich and delicious, but also a Yin-nourishing tonic. When cooking, you must first peel off its black skin in boiling water. There are two ways to eat it. Boiling it with ham is fresh and delicious, but braising it with fresh meat is even more greasy and delicious. It is said that the red belly of soft-shelled turtles is transformed from snakes, and it is poisonous and inedible.

Yellow Croaker Yellow croaker, also known as summer fish, is cooked and eaten by every household in Suzhou on the day of Lichun to celebrate the season. The meat of yellow croaker is fresh and delicious, and there are very few fish bones, which makes it easier to eat. There are two sizes of yellow croaker, produced in the South China Sea in Zhejiang. When the spring river warms, the fish come in droves from the south, and at this time, the fishing boats go to catch them in groups. The simplest way to eat yellow croaker is to stew it with soy sauce and wine; it can also be braised. Braised, remove the fish bones, cook it into fish soup, and cook it with noodles, it is really delicious!

Hilsa Herring Hilsa herring is produced in the Yangtze River in Changshu and Zhenjiang, and there is also production in the head of the Fuchun River in Zhejiang. Hilsa herring is an indispensable seasonal delicacy in the Dragon Boat Festival gifts of Jiangnan families. Often the fish has changed its taste, but it is still carried around by servants. The way to eat hilsa herring is mostly to stew it with South Leg and lard. There is a lot of fat under its scales, so you don't remove the scales when you eat it, which is a special thing about eating fish. Hilsa herring is precious and fresh, so people who are particular about eating often go to the bottom of Jinshan to wait for the hilsa herring to come out of the water and cook it immediately. It is said that there is a kind of fragrance in the freshness, which ordinary hilsa herring cannot compare; because the hilsa herring dies as soon as it leaves the water, it must be cooked and eaten on the spot.

Cocktail fish Cocktail fish is also a fresh fish that is on the market in early summer. Its shape is like a small puffer fish, yellow with black spots; the white belly can swell very large, and it is smooth and delicate. When eating cocktail fish, you must tear off the fish skin. The lungs of the cocktail fish are very delicious. When it is first on the market, it is like broad beans, tender, fat, and fresh, and melts in your mouth, which is indeed a special flavor. Mr. Yu Youren was greatly inspired by poetry when he ate cocktail lung soup at the Shijia Hotel in Mudu, and wrote a poem of praise on the wall; later, because Li Genyuan first changed "cocktail" to "魞", Mr. Yu was very dissatisfied, and he rewrote his poem on paper and sent it to Shijia, leaving a romantic story in Mudu to this day. 鮝鱼 The taste of 鮝鱼 is very salty, and it is the most appetizing dish in the meal. The way to eat it is to stew it, braise it, both are not bad; cooking it with flour is even more delicious. The fish bones on the head of the 鮝鱼 can be made into a flying crane, and it is as delicate as the crab and butterfly.

In addition to the above types, there are also "Exam Fish" and "Squid" in early summer. "Fishing in the water is fresh and edible," which is enough for gourmets to feast on. However, when I write here, I suddenly think of a story about fish; "The Song City gate caught fire, and the people rescued it. They fetched water from the pond to put out the fire. When the water dried up, all the fish in the pond died." When enemy planes are flying around Peiping and the northeast fan barrier is completely lost, we ordinary people will one day be the fish in the pond that will suffer. But looking around the country, young people are saving the country by dancing, businessmen are saving the country by prostitution, and 乂乂们乂乂 are saving the country by opium, and gambling to save the country, and are still swimming in the cauldron with burning firewood. Except for listening to being fish and meat on the table, and being slaughtered by others, what way out is there! It's really going to be the sentence "Am I a fish?"
