Silk and Tea

Combined Records of Both Silk Cocoon Markets

(Supply of High-Quality Yuyao Cocoons Increasingly Scarce)

New Yuyao cocoons have been on the market for over a week. This year's breeding varies, and cocoon production is still low. The quality of improved varieties is the best, and various firms are competing to purchase high-quality cocoons. The supply has become increasingly scarce in the past two days. The highest cocoon price is $40, and the lowest is $25.

(Xinchang Cocoon Market Nears End)

The cocoon shops have been open for almost ten days, and inspections are strict. The market is preparing to close due to recent poor quality deliveries. The average cocoon price for this session is expected to be around $30.

(Sheng County Cocoon Production Only 30-40%)

Not many people are breeding foreign varieties this year. There was a sudden change in weather during the major sleep, causing 40% to be abandoned. The overall cocoon harvest in the entire county is only 30-40%. The cocoon price for improved high-quality cocoons is $35-$40, and native varieties are $25-$26.

(Few Danyang Cocoon Shops Open)

Only about ten cocoon shops are open. The shops have been open for three days, and the market supply is not strong. The cocoon price for improved varieties is $32.30-$34.50, and native varieties are $24.50-$26.70.

(Yangzhong New Cocoon Harvest Is Difficult to Be Abundant)

Farmers in the riverside markets and villages of Yangzhong have suffered damage to their native silkworms bred by Changbang this year. The remaining silkworms are limited, and the number of improved varieties bred as replacements is also small. The cocoon harvest is unlikely to be abundant. New cocoons have already been on the market. It is estimated that the overall new cocoon harvest for this session will be only 40-50% of a normal year. The cocoon price is $25-$26, and improved high-quality cocoons are $30-$32.

(Chenri Silk Factory Actively Declares Shipments)

The Min group purchased 100 bags of Hunan machine oil at $8.30, 550 bags of rough oil at $7.50-$7.40, 400 bags of rough Jing at $6.78, and 700+ bags of Nanjing Che Indica at $7.75. Medium and low grades were sold at correspondingly lower prices, and the goods that were sold were not particularly high quality.

New Rapeseed Futures Already Thrown Open

Oilseed Cakes Highly Sought After

New rapeseed from various ports has already appeared this year, but it has not yet been shipped to Shanghai, due to the impact of the price not meeting expectations. Producers and 车坊 (car workshop) in the producing areas have successively started operations, but there has been no shipment to Shanghai yet. It is currently heard that 2,000 packages of the July futures were thrown open with the price at 5 Liang. Oilseed cakes are enjoying the soaring market prices, and the local market has an upright mentality. The market atmosphere is swaying straight upwards. The biscuit market is flatter than the oil market. Medium quality yellow soybeans have increased the fastest. It is temporarily difficult to predict whether the future will go up or down.

Hardware　Water Cement Still Looks Bullish

Since the price increase of water cement, buyers are still very enthusiastic. Due to various environmental factors, manufacturers are still looking at a bullish market. Yesterday, the estimated price for the "Horse" brand was $7.30, and the "Elephant" brand was $7.35. For large transactions, there is still no spot stock. Because of this, construction workers are complaining because they cannot purchase any stock.

Galvanized Iron Sheets Practically Frozen

Judging from past years, galvanized iron sheet sales should be at their peak right now. However, due to the extremely tight monetary situation this year and the impact of the war in the north, sales have decreased significantly. Business for local construction workers and factories is also stagnant. Yesterday's market price for standard size 24 was only $14.70 per dan (unit), size 26 was $15.35, and size 28 was $17.00. Transactions were only sporadic.

Discussions

The Attitude That Young People Should Have Now

— Jin Zhi

Youth is both admirable and despicable; youth can have pure thoughts or base thoughts. Youth can go astray and do evil, and youth can be the most passionate in sacrificing themselves. In short, everything about youth exists between the adorable and the detestable, and the power of youth to shift the course of human society toward evolution or devolution is the greatest.

Most people think that the future happiness of humankind must be sought by young people, and the future peaceful paradise must be created by young people. Young people are pure and have conscience. In this view, young people are full of hope, and their responsibilities are of utmost importance. Young people will undoubtedly speak with honesty and purity and do things with integrity and justice. However, the current state of society is truly diverse and full of strange things. Although old bad habits and evil forces are flashing back with a dying glow and brandishing their claws, most ambitious young people may not pay attention to them. However, "false words and eloquence, non-compliant actions and eccentricity," the happiness and liberalism, are indeed the greatest enemies of young people. They are also the tempters of young people, exploiting the weaknesses of youth's indulgence and desire for quick success and instant benefits, using money and beauty to dazzle them. Moreover, the "greedy and insatiable" Japanese also exploit young people's weakness of wanting to get promoted and get rich, to bewitch them into becoming traitors, making them listen with fascination, and wholeheartedly offering themselves up for exploitation. Even if they die, they will have no regrets, as long as they can cause chaos and carry out Japanese policies, they can get promoted and get rich. If young people step onto this path of delusion, who wouldn't be overjoyed, thinking that they are enjoying all the blessings of the world and becoming the king of power in the human world? However, we, the young people who pride ourselves on having a conscience, who claim to have pure and clean thoughts, do we all agree that this is right? Is this considered a social revolution? If we acknowledge it, then we are already running down the path of evil, leading the country towards national ruin and the society towards regression!

The aspirations that we young people should have should be great and universal, hoping that everyone will engage in productive work, so that all humankind can live in freedom, equality, and happiness. All people in the world should develop their innate abilities, and all people in the world should have permanent mutual assistance and universal love, creating a world of ultimate bliss. This is the great path that we young people should take. All current forms of plunder and power are regressive and inhumane. Therefore, as a current youth, I must maintain an attitude of careful study and research. Climbing a mountain requires walking step by step, while jumping into the water requires only one leap. Therefore, we must not only be willing to sacrifice for the truth, but also have a firm and patient attitude that is not confused by short-term gains and small benefits.

Random Notes on Fundraising

— Qi Ling

For the sake of aviation to save the country through donations, the Boy Scouts of various schools have set off to serve. And so, I am also one of the members of a certain school.

On a breezy and clear morning, our team of six, carrying flags, donation boxes, and receipt books, set off with great enthusiasm.

"Sir! Please donate as you wish."

The first person we encountered was a middle-aged merchant, and we stopped him.

"Okay!" Then a silver dollar was dropped into our donation box. He seemed very generous.

We walked into the back door of a certain house.

"What are you doing? Who are you looking for?" An old woman with gray hair showed a panic expression on her face when she saw us uninvited guests.

"We are students, because our China wants to buy airplanes to fight the Japanese, so we are out fundraising. Old lady! Would you be willing to donate something here?" I quickly explained to her.

"What? Are you fundraising again? Wasn't there fundraising when the revolutionary army was fighting before? No, no."

"Donate as much as you want, whatever you can." Old Wu said.

"Alright, alright, take these four copper coins, what a bother."

The old woman dropped four copper coins into my hand. "Four copper coins!" I thought. But it was not good to refuse.

Literature and Art

Sentiments

— Jin Zhi

Reading the newspaper for consecutive days fills me with tears,

Every page proclaims the sound of national crisis.

The Communist bandits spread and invade Jiangxi Province,

The Japanese bandits rage and press on Beijing.

The disaster victims' blood and sweat are exhausted in the entire region,

The bones of brave warriors lie scattered across the fields.

Looking back at those officials whose pockets are privately full,

They are too heartless to contribute even a hair.

News of war losses makes my dreams fearful,

I hate that I don't have a swift sword to cut down the long whale.

Indecision loses us thousands of miles of land,

Aggressors swallow up four provinces.

Relying on the League of Nations, they are all afraid to die,

Requesting the government, they also steal life.

Why not unite with all our comrades,

And strive to support the front in Beiping.

"Good young people, instead of staying in school and studying peacefully, they insist on running around, fundraising for what?" We still heard the old woman mumbling indistinctly as we left the gate.

We then encountered a young man dressed in fancy clothes.

"Please donate, sir!"

"What will you use the donations for?" he said with a smile.

"Sir, don't you know? This time we are raising money for the aviation to save the country fund. Haven't you seen the news in the newspapers?" I said with a tone of contempt.

"You also want me to donate something, right?"

"Yes, as much as you want." Old Wang replied.

"Oh! I have money, but I won't donate. Are you going to scold me for being a cold-blooded animal?"

"..." We thought this person was mentally ill.

"You bunch of..." He said indifferently: "Aviation to save the country fund, let me ask you, will the money you donate be used to buy airplanes? Will you be able to fly the airplanes yourselves? Old [I] say, before you set out to fundraise, Shanghai
